<?php
if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

// Check current user capabilities
if (!current_user_can('manage_options')) {
    wp_die(__('You do not have sufficient permissions to access this page.'));
}

// Handle form submission
if ($_POST && check_admin_referer('aimagic_settings')) {
    $settings = [
        'api_keys' => [
            'openai' => sanitize_text_field($_POST['openai_api_key']),
            'google' => sanitize_text_field($_POST['google_api_key']),
            'azure' => sanitize_text_field($_POST['azure_api_key'])
        ],
        'endpoints' => [
            'openai' => esc_url_raw($_POST['openai_endpoint']),
            'google' => esc_url_raw($_POST['google_endpoint']),
            'azure' => esc_url_raw($_POST['azure_endpoint'])
        ],
        'limits' => [
            'max_tokens' => intval($_POST['max_tokens']),
            'max_requests' => intval($_POST['max_requests']),
            'max_storage' => intval($_POST['max_storage'])
        ],
        'defaults' => [
            'model' => sanitize_text_field($_POST['default_model']),
            'language' => sanitize_text_field($_POST['default_language']),
            'temperature' => floatval($_POST['temperature'])
        ],
        'security' => [
            'require_auth' => isset($_POST['require_auth']),
            'allowed_domains' => array_map('sanitize_text_field', explode("\n", $_POST['allowed_domains'])),
            'rate_limit' => intval($_POST['rate_limit'])
        ],
        'monitoring' => [
            'enable_logging' => isset($_POST['enable_logging']),
            'log_retention' => intval($_POST['log_retention']),
            'alert_threshold' => intval($_POST['alert_threshold']),
            'notify_email' => sanitize_email($_POST['notify_email'])
        ],
        'webhooks' => [
            'success_url' => esc_url_raw($_POST['success_webhook']),
            'error_url' => esc_url_raw($_POST['error_webhook']),
            'timeout' => intval($_POST['webhook_timeout'])
        ],
        'cache' => [
            'enable_cache' => isset($_POST['enable_cache']),
            'cache_duration' => intval($_POST['cache_duration']),
            'max_cache_size' => intval($_POST['max_cache_size'])
        ],
        'optimization' => [
            'batch_size' => intval($_POST['batch_size']),
            'parallel_requests' => intval($_POST['parallel_requests']),
            'retry_attempts' => intval($_POST['retry_attempts'])
        ]
    ];

    update_option('aimagic_settings', $settings);
    echo '<div class="updated"><p>' . __('Settings saved successfully.', 'aimagic') . '</p></div>';
}

<script type="text/javascript">
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    // Handle password visibility toggle
    $('.toggle-password').click(function() {
        var $input = $(this).prev('input');
        var type = $input.attr('type') === 'password' ? 'text' : 'password';
        $input.attr('type', type);
    });

    // Handle temperature slider
    var $temperature = $('#temperature');
    var $temperatureValue = $('#temperature-value');
    
    function updateTemperature() {
        $temperatureValue.text($temperature.val());
    }
    
    $temperature.on('input', updateTemperature);
    updateTemperature();

    // Handle form submission
    $('form').submit(function() {
        var confirmed = true;
        
        // Check if API keys are empty
        $('.settings-section input[type="password"]').each(function() {
            if (!$(this).val() && !confirmed) {
                confirmed = confirm('<?php _e('Some API keys are empty. Continue anyway?', 'aimagic'); ?>');
                return false;
            }
        });

        return confirmed;
    });

    // Test API connections
    function testApiConnection(provider) {
        var $button = $('#test-' + provider);
        var $status = $('#' + provider + '-status');
        
        $button.prop('disabled', true).text('Testing...');
        $status.html('');

        $.ajax({
            url: ajaxurl,
            method: 'POST',
            data: {
                action: 'test_api_connection',
                provider: provider,
                api_key: $('#' + provider + '_api_key').val(),
                endpoint: $('#' + provider + '_endpoint').val(),
                nonce: '<?php echo wp_create_nonce('test_api_connection'); ?>'
            },
            success: function(response) {
                if (response.success) {
                    $status.html('<span class="success">✓ Connected</span>');
                } else {
                    $status.html('<span class="error">✗ ' + response.data + '</span>');
                }
            },
            error: function() {
                $status.html('<span class="error">✗ Connection failed</span>');
            },
            complete: function() {
                $button.prop('disabled', false).text('Test Connection');
            }
        });
    }

    // Add test buttons for each provider
    $('.settings-section h3').each(function() {
        var provider = $(this).text().toLowerCase().replace(' ai', '');
        $(this).after(
            '<button type="button" class="button" id="test-' + provider + '">Test Connection</button>' +
            '<span id="' + provider + '-status" style="margin-left: 10px;"></span>'
        );
        
        $('#test-' + provider).click(function() {
            testApiConnection(provider);
        });
    });
});
</script>

目錄：/www/wwwroot/xart004.heatgroups.top/wp-content/plugins/ai_plateform_v2/files_2025/admin/views
檔名：admin-payments.php
==================================================
<?php
if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

// Check current user capabilities
if (!current_user_can('manage_options')) {
    wp_die(__('You do not have sufficient permissions to access this page.'));
}

// Load the Payments List Table class
require_once AIMAGIC_PLUGIN_DIR . 'includes/admin/class-admin-payments-list.php';

// Create an instance of our list table
$payments_list_table = new AIMagic\Admin\Payments_List_Table();
$payments_list_table->prepare_items();
?>

<div class="wrap">
    <h1 class="wp-heading-inline"><?php _e('Payments', 'aimagic'); ?></h1>
    <a href="<?php echo admin_url('admin.php?page=aimagic-payments&action=add'); ?>" class="page-title-action">
        <?php _e('Add Manual Payment', 'aimagic'); ?>
    </a>
    <hr class="wp-header-end">

    <!-- Dashboard Cards -->
    <div class="aimagic-dashboard-cards">
        <?php
        global $wpdb;
        
        // Get payment statistics
        $stats = $wpdb->get_row("
            SELECT 
                COUNT(*) as total_transactions,
                SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'completed' THEN amount ELSE 0 END) as total_revenue,
                SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'pending' THEN amount ELSE 0 END) as pending_amount,
                COUNT(CASE WHEN created_at >= DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 30 DAY) THEN 1 END) as monthly_transactions
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_payments
        ");
        ?>
        <div class="card">
            <h3><?php _e('Total Revenue', 'aimagic'); ?></h3>
            <p class="amount"><?php echo number_format_i18n($stats->total_revenue, 2); ?></p>
        </div>
        <div class="card">
            <h3><?php _e('Pending Amount', 'aimagic'); ?></h3>
            <p class="amount"><?php echo number_format_i18n($stats->pending_amount, 2); ?></p>
        </div>
        <div class="card">
            <h3><?php _e('Monthly Transactions', 'aimagic'); ?></h3>

<script type="text/javascript">
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    // Handle date range validation
    $('#filter-date-from, #filter-date-to').change(function() {
        var fromDate = $('#filter-date-from').val();
        var toDate = $('#filter-date-to').val();
        
        if (fromDate && toDate && fromDate > toDate) {
            alert('<?php _e('From date cannot be later than To date', 'aimagic'); ?>');
            $(this).val('');
        }
    });

    // Handle export CSV
    $('#export_csv').click(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var queryParams = {
            action: 'export_payments_csv',
            status: $('#filter-by-status').val(),
            payment_method: $('#filter-by-method').val(),
            date_from: $('#filter-date-from').val(),
            date_to: $('#filter-date-to').val(),
            search: $('#search_payments').val(),
            nonce: '<?php echo wp_create_nonce('export_payments_csv'); ?>'
        };
        
        window.location.href = ajaxurl + '?' + $.param(queryParams);
    });

    // Initialize datepicker for date filters
    $('.datepicker').datepicker({
        dateFormat: 'yy-mm-dd',
        maxDate: '0'
    });

    // Real-time amount formatting
    function formatAmount(input) {
        var value = input.value.replace(/[^\d.]/g, '');
        var parts = value.split('.');
        parts[0] = parts[0].replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ',');
        if (parts.length > 1) {
            parts[1] = parts[1].substring(0, 2);
        }
        input.value = parts.join('.');
    }

    $('input.amount').on('input', function() {
        formatAmount(this);
    });
});
</script>

檔名：class-users-list.php

<?php
namespace AIMagic\Admin\Lists;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

if (!class_exists('WP_List_Table')) {
    require_once(ABSPATH . 'wp-admin/includes/class-wp-list-table.php');
}

class UsersList extends \WP_List_Table {
    /**
     * Constructor.
     */
    public function __construct() {
        parent::__construct([
            'singular' => 'user',
            'plural'   => 'users',
            'ajax'     => false
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Get columns.
     */
    public function get_columns() {
        return [
            'cb'            => '<input type="checkbox" />',
            'username'      => __('Username', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'tenant'        => __('Tenant', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'quota_usage'   => __('Quota Usage', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'tasks'         => __('Tasks', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'last_active'   => __('Last Active', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'status'        => __('Status', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Get sortable columns.
     */
    public function get_sortable_columns() {
        return [
            'username'     => ['user_login', true],
            'tenant'       => ['tenant_id', false],
            'quota_usage'  => ['quota_used', false],
            'tasks'        => ['task_count', false],
            'last_active'  => ['last_active', false],
            'status'       => ['status', false]
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Prepare items.
     */
    public function prepare_items() {
        global $wpdb;

        // Set up pagination
        $per_page = 20;
        $current_page = $this->get_pagenum();

        // Build query
        $where = [];
        $values = [];

        if (!empty($_REQUEST['tenant_id'])) {
            $where[] = 'au.tenant_id = %d';
            $values[] = intval($_REQUEST['tenant_id']);
        }

        if (!empty($_REQUEST['status'])) {
            $where[] = 'au.status = %s';
            $values[] = sanitize_text_field($_REQUEST['status']);
        }

        if (!empty($_REQUEST['s'])) {
            $search = '%' . $wpdb->esc_like($_REQUEST['s']) . '%';
            $where[] = '(u.user_login LIKE %s OR u.user_email LIKE %s OR u.display_name LIKE %s)';
            $values[] = $search;
            $values[] = $search;
            $values[] = $search;
        }

        $where_clause = !empty($where) ? 'WHERE ' . implode(' AND ', $where) : '';

        // Get total items
        $total_items = $wpdb->get_var($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT au.id)
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_users au
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->users} u ON au.user_id = u.ID
            $where_clause",
            $values
        ));

        // Get items
        $orderby = isset($_REQUEST['orderby']) ? $_REQUEST['orderby'] : 'last_active';
        $order = isset($_REQUEST['order']) ? $_REQUEST['order'] : 'DESC';

        $this->items = $wpdb->get_results($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT au.*,
                u.user_login,
                u.user_email,
                u.display_name,
                t.name as tenant_name,
                COUNT(tk.id) as task_count,
                MAX(tk.created_at) as last_task_date
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_users au
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->users} u ON au.user_id = u.ID
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants t ON au.tenant_id = t.id
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks tk ON au.id = tk.user_id
            $where_clause
            GROUP BY au.id
            ORDER BY $orderby $order
            LIMIT %d OFFSET %d",
            array_merge($values, [$per_page, ($current_page - 1) * $per_page])
        ));

        // Set pagination args
        $this->set_pagination_args([
            'total_items' => $total_items,
            'per_page'    => $per_page,
            'total_pages' => ceil($total_items / $per_page)
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Column default.
     */
    public function column_default($item, $column_name) {
        switch ($column_name) {
            case 'tenant':
                return sprintf(
                    '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tenants&action=view&id=' . $item->tenant_id),
                    esc_html($item->tenant_name)
                );
            case 'quota_usage':
                return $this->get_quota_usage_html($item);
            case 'tasks':
                return sprintf(
                    '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tasks&user_id=' . $item->user_id),
                    number_format_i18n($item->task_count)
                );
            case 'last_active':
                $last_active = max(strtotime($item->last_active), strtotime($item->last_task_date));
                return $last_active ? sprintf(
                    _x('%s ago', '%s = human-readable time difference', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    human_time_diff($last_active, current_time('timestamp'))
                ) : __('Never', 'ai-magic-publisher');
            case 'status':
                return $this->get_status_html($item->status);
            default:
                return print_r($item, true);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Column username.
     */
    public function column_username($item) {
        $actions = [
            'edit' => sprintf(
                '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-users&action=edit&id=' . $item->id),
                __('Edit', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            ),
            'view' => sprintf(
                '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-users&action=view&id=' . $item->id),
                __('View Details', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            ),
            'reset_quota' => sprintf(
                '<a href="#" class="reset-quota" data-user-id="%d">%s</a>',
                $item->id,
                __('Reset Quota', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            )
        ];

        if ($item->status === 'active') {
            $actions['suspend'] = sprintf(
                '<a href="%s" class="suspend-user">%s</a>',
                wp_nonce_url(
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-users&action=suspend&id=' . $item->id),
                    'suspend_user_' . $item->id
                ),
                __('Suspend', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            );
        } else {
            $actions['activate'] = sprintf(
                '<a href="%s" class="activate-user">%s</a>',
                wp_nonce_url(
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-users&action=activate&id=' . $item->id),
                    'activate_user_' . $item->id
                ),
                __('Activate', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            );
        }

        $user_display = sprintf(
            '<strong>%s</strong><br /><span class="user-email">%s</span>',
            esc_html($item->display_name),
            esc_html($item->user_email)
        );

        return sprintf('%1$s %2$s', $user_display, $this->row_actions($actions));
    }

    /**
     * Get bulk actions.
     */
    public function get_bulk_actions() {
        return [
            'activate'     => __('Activate', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'suspend'      => __('Suspend', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'reset_quota'  => __('Reset Quota', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'delete'       => __('Delete', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Column cb.
     */
    public function column_cb($item) {
        return sprintf(
            '<input type="checkbox" name="users[]" value="%s" />',
            $item->id
        );
    }

    /**
     * Get quota usage HTML.
     */
    private function get_quota_usage_html($item) {
        $percentage = $item->quota_limit > 0 ? 
            ($item->quota_used / $item->quota_limit) * 100 : 0;

        $class = 'quota-normal';
        if ($percentage >= 90) {
            $class = 'quota-critical';
        } elseif ($percentage >= 70) {
            $class = 'quota-warning';
        }

        return sprintf(
            '<div class="quota-usage %s">
                <div class="quota-bar">
                    <div class="quota-bar-fill" style="width: %d%%"></div>
                </div>
                <div class="quota-text">%s / %s</div>
            </div>',
            esc_attr($class),
            min(100, $percentage),
            size_format($item->quota_used),
            $item->quota_limit > 0 ? size_format($item->quota_limit) : __('Unlimited', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        );
    }

    /**
     * Get status HTML.
     */
    private function get_status_html($status) {
        $statuses = [
            'active'    => ['label' => __('Active', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-active'],
            'inactive'  => ['label' => __('Inactive', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-inactive'],
            'suspended' => ['label' => __('Suspended', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-suspended']
        ];

        return isset($statuses[$status]) ? sprintf(
            '<span class="%s">%s</span>',
            esc_attr($statuses[$status]['class']),
            esc_html($statuses[$status]['label'])
        ) : esc_html($status);
    }

    /**
     * Process bulk action.
     */
    public function process_bulk_action() {
        $action = $this->current_action();
        if (!$action) return;

        $user_ids = isset($_REQUEST['users']) ? array_map('intval', $_REQUEST['users']) : [];
        if (empty($user_ids)) return;

        switch ($action) {
            case 'activate':
                foreach ($user_ids as $user_id) {
                    update_user_status($user_id, 'active');
                }
                break;

            case 'suspend':
                foreach ($user_ids as $user_id) {
                    update_user_status($user_id, 'suspended');
                }
                break;

            case 'reset_quota':
                foreach ($user_ids as $user_id) {
                    reset_user_quota($user_id);
                }
                break;

            case 'delete':
                foreach ($user_ids as $user_id) {
                    delete_aimagic_user($user_id);
                }
                break;
        }

        wp_redirect(add_query_arg('message', $action . 'd', wp_get_referer()));
        exit;
    }
}

目錄：/www/wwwroot/xart004.heatgroups.top/wp-content/plugins/ai_plateform_v2/files_2025/admin/lists
檔名：class-tenants-list.php

<?php
namespace AIMagic\Admin\Lists;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

if (!class_exists('WP_List_Table')) {
    require_once(ABSPATH . 'wp-admin/includes/class-wp-list-table.php');
}

class TenantsList extends \WP_List_Table {
    /**
     * Constructor.
     */
    public function __construct() {
        parent::__construct([
            'singular' => 'tenant',
            'plural'   => 'tenants',
            'ajax'     => false
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Get columns.
     */
    public function get_columns() {
        return [
            'cb'          => '<input type="checkbox" />',
            'name'        => __('Name', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'api_key'     => __('API Key', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'users'       => __('Users', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'tasks'       => __('Tasks', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'quota_usage' => __('Quota Usage', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'status'      => __('Status', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'created_at'  => __('Created', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Get sortable columns.
     */
    public function get_sortable_columns() {
        return [
            'name'       => ['name', true],
            'users'      => ['users', false],
            'tasks'      => ['tasks', false],
            'status'     => ['status', false],
            'created_at' => ['created_at', false]
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Prepare items.
     */
    public function prepare_items() {
        global $wpdb;

        // Set up pagination
        $per_page = 20;
        $current_page = $this->get_pagenum();
        $total_items = $wpdb->get_var("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants");

        // Set up ordering
        $orderby = isset($_REQUEST['orderby']) ? trim($_REQUEST['orderby']) : 'created_at';
        $order = isset($_REQUEST['order']) ? trim($_REQUEST['order']) : 'DESC';

        // Get items
        $this->items = $wpdb->get_results($wpdb->prepare("
            SELECT t.*,
                COUNT(DISTINCT u.id) as user_count,
                COUNT(DISTINCT tk.id) as task_count,
                SUM(u.quota_used) as total_quota_used
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants t
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_users u ON t.id = u.tenant_id
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks tk ON t.id = tk.tenant_id
            GROUP BY t.id
            ORDER BY {$orderby} {$order}
            LIMIT %d OFFSET %d",
            $per_page,
            ($current_page - 1) * $per_page
        ));

        // Set pagination args
        $this->set_pagination_args([
            'total_items' => $total_items,
            'per_page'    => $per_page,
            'total_pages' => ceil($total_items / $per_page)
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Column default.
     */
    public function column_default($item, $column_name) {
        switch ($column_name) {
            case 'api_key':
                return sprintf(
                    '<code class="api-key">%s</code> 
                    <button type="button" class="button copy-api-key" data-api-key="%s">%s</button>',
                    $this->mask_api_key($item->api_key),
                    esc_attr($item->api_key),
                    __('Copy', 'ai-magic-publisher')
                );
            case 'users':
                return sprintf(
                    '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-users&tenant_id=' . $item->id),
                    number_format_i18n($item->user_count)
                );
            case 'tasks':
                return sprintf(
                    '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tasks&tenant_id=' . $item->id),
                    number_format_i18n($item->task_count)
                );
            case 'quota_usage':
                return $this->get_quota_usage_html($item);
            case 'status':
                return $this->get_status_html($item->status);
            case 'created_at':
                return wp_date(
                    get_option('date_format') . ' ' . get_option('time_format'),
                    strtotime($item->created_at)
                );
            default:
                return print_r($item, true);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Column name.
     */
    public function column_name($item) {
        $actions = [
            'edit' => sprintf(
                '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tenants&action=edit&id=' . $item->id),
                __('Edit', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            ),
            'view' => sprintf(
                '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tenants&action=view&id=' . $item->id),
                __('View Details', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            )
        ];

        if ($item->status === 'active') {
            $actions['deactivate'] = sprintf(
                '<a href="%s" class="toggle-tenant-status" data-tenant-id="%d" data-new-status="inactive">%s</a>',
                wp_nonce_url(
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tenants&action=deactivate&id=' . $item->id),
                    'deactivate_tenant_' . $item->id
                ),
                $item->id,
                __('Deactivate', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            );
        } else {
            $actions['activate'] = sprintf(
                '<a href="%s" class="toggle-tenant-status" data-tenant-id="%d" data-new-status="active">%s</a>',
                wp_nonce_url(
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tenants&action=activate&id=' . $item->id),
                    'activate_tenant_' . $item->id
                ),
                $item->id,
                __('Activate', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            );
        }

        return sprintf(
            '%1$s %2$s',
            '<strong>' . esc_html($item->name) . '</strong>',
            $this->row_actions($actions)
        );
    }

    /**
     * Get bulk actions.
     */
    public function get_bulk_actions() {
        return [
            'activate'   => __('Activate', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'deactivate' => __('Deactivate', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'delete'     => __('Delete', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Column cb.
     */
    public function column_cb($item) {
        return sprintf(
            '<input type="checkbox" name="tenants[]" value="%s" />',
            $item->id
        );
    }

    /**
     * Get status HTML.
     */
    private function get_status_html($status) {
        $statuses = [
            'active'    => ['label' => __('Active', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-active'],
            'inactive'  => ['label' => __('Inactive', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-inactive'],
            'suspended' => ['label' => __('Suspended', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-suspended']
        ];

        return isset($statuses[$status]) ? sprintf(
            '<span class="%s">%s</span>',
            esc_attr($statuses[$status]['class']),
            esc_html($statuses[$status]['label'])
        ) : esc_html($status);
    }

    /**
     * Get quota usage HTML.
     */
    private function get_quota_usage_html($item) {
        $quota_limit = get_tenant_quota_limit($item->id);
        $percentage = $quota_limit > 0 ? ($item->total_quota_used / $quota_limit) * 100 : 0;
        
        return sprintf(
            '<div class="quota-usage">
                <div class="quota-bar">
                    <div class="quota-bar-fill" style="width: %d%%"></div>
                </div>
                <div class="quota-text">%s / %s</div>
            </div>',
            min(100, $percentage),
            size_format($item->total_quota_used),
            $quota_limit > 0 ? size_format($quota_limit) : __('Unlimited', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        );
    }

    /**
     * Mask API key.
     */
    private function mask_api_key($key) {
        if (strlen($key) <= 8) return str_repeat('•', strlen($key));
        return substr($key, 0, 4) . str_repeat('•', strlen($key) - 8) . substr($key, -4);
    }

    /**
     * Process bulk actions.
     */
    public function process_bulk_action() {
        $action = $this->current_action();
        if (!$action) return;

        $tenant_ids = isset($_REQUEST['tenants']) ? array_map('intval', $_REQUEST['tenants']) : [];
        if (empty($tenant_ids)) return;

        switch ($action) {
            case 'activate':
            case 'deactivate':
                foreach ($tenant_ids as $tenant_id) {
                    update_tenant_status($tenant_id, $action === 'activate' ? 'active' : 'inactive');
                }
                break;

            case 'delete':
                foreach ($tenant_ids as $tenant_id) {
                    delete_tenant($tenant_id);
                }
                break;
        }

        wp_redirect(add_query_arg('message', $action . 'd', wp_get_referer()));
        exit;
    }
}

<?php
namespace AIMagic\Admin\Lists;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

if (!class_exists('WP_List_Table')) {
    require_once(ABSPATH . 'wp-admin/includes/class-wp-list-table.php');
}

class TasksList extends \WP_List_Table {
    /**
     * Constructor.
     */
    public function __construct() {
        parent::__construct([
            'singular' => 'task',
            'plural'   => 'tasks',
            'ajax'     => false
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Get columns.
     */
    public function get_columns() {
        return [
            'cb'          => '<input type="checkbox" />',
            'id'          => __('ID', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'type'        => __('Type', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'tenant'      => __('Tenant', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'user'        => __('User', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'status'      => __('Status', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'created_at'  => __('Created', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'completed_at' => __('Completed', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Get sortable columns.
     */
    public function get_sortable_columns() {
        return [
            'id'          => ['id', true],
            'type'        => ['type', false],
            'tenant'      => ['tenant_id', false],
            'status'      => ['status', false],
            'created_at'  => ['created_at', false],
            'completed_at' => ['completed_at', false]
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Prepare items.
     */
    public function prepare_items() {
        global $wpdb;

        // Set up pagination
        $per_page = 20;
        $current_page = $this->get_pagenum();

        // Build query
        $where = [];
        $values = [];

        if (!empty($_REQUEST['tenant_id'])) {
            $where[] = 't.tenant_id = %d';
            $values[] = intval($_REQUEST['tenant_id']);
        }

        if (!empty($_REQUEST['user_id'])) {
            $where[] = 't.user_id = %d';
            $values[] = intval($_REQUEST['user_id']);
        }

        if (!empty($_REQUEST['status'])) {
            $where[] = 't.status = %s';
            $values[] = sanitize_text_field($_REQUEST['status']);
        }

        if (!empty($_REQUEST['type'])) {
            $where[] = 't.type = %s';
            $values[] = sanitize_text_field($_REQUEST['type']);
        }

        $where_clause = !empty($where) ? 'WHERE ' . implode(' AND ', $where) : '';

        // Get total items
        $total_items = $wpdb->get_var($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT COUNT(*)
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks t
            $where_clause",
            $values
        ));

        // Get items
        $orderby = isset($_REQUEST['orderby']) ? $_REQUEST['orderby'] : 'created_at';
        $order = isset($_REQUEST['order']) ? $_REQUEST['order'] : 'DESC';

        $this->items = $wpdb->get_results($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT t.*,
                tn.name as tenant_name,
                u.display_name as user_name
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks t
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants tn ON t.tenant_id = tn.id
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->users} u ON t.user_id = u.ID
            $where_clause
            ORDER BY $orderby $order
            LIMIT %d OFFSET %d",
            array_merge($values, [$per_page, ($current_page - 1) * $per_page])
        ));

        // Set pagination args
        $this->set_pagination_args([
            'total_items' => $total_items,
            'per_page'    => $per_page,
            'total_pages' => ceil($total_items / $per_page)
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Column default.
     */
    public function column_default($item, $column_name) {
        switch ($column_name) {
            case 'id':
                return '#' . $item->id;
            case 'type':
                return $this->get_task_type_label($item->type);
            case 'tenant':
                return sprintf(
                    '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tenants&action=view&id=' . $item->tenant_id),
                    esc_html($item->tenant_name)
                );
            case 'user':
                return sprintf(
                    '<a href="%s">%s</a>',
                    admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-users&action=view&id=' . $item->user_id),
                    esc_html($item->user_name)
                );
            case 'status':
                return $this->get_status_html($item->status);
            case 'created_at':
            case 'completed_at':
                return $item->$column_name ? wp_date(
                    get_option('date_format') . ' ' . get_option('time_format'),
                    strtotime($item->$column_name)
                ) : '—';
            default:
                return print_r($item, true);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Column cb.
     */
    public function column_cb($item) {
        return sprintf(
            '<input type="checkbox" name="tasks[]" value="%s" />',
            $item->id
        );
    }

    /**
     * Get bulk actions.
     */
    public function get_bulk_actions() {
        return [
            'retry'   => __('Retry', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'cancel'  => __('Cancel', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'delete'  => __('Delete', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Process bulk action.
     */
    public function process_bulk_action() {
        $action = $this->current_action();
        if (!$action) return;

        $task_ids = isset($_REQUEST['tasks']) ? array_map('intval', $_REQUEST['tasks']) : [];
        if (empty($task_ids)) return;

        switch ($action) {
            case 'retry':
                foreach ($task_ids as $task_id) {
                    retry_task($task_id);
                }
                break;

            case 'cancel':
                foreach ($task_ids as $task_id) {
                    cancel_task($task_id);
                }
                break;

            case 'delete':
                foreach ($task_ids as $task_id) {
                    delete_task($task_id);
                }
                break;
        }

        wp_redirect(add_query_arg('message', $action . 'd', wp_get_referer()));
        exit;
    }

    /**
     * Get task type label.
     */
    private function get_task_type_label($type) {
        $types = [
            'content_generation' => __('Content Generation', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'image_generation'   => __('Image Generation', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'translation'        => __('Translation', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'summarization'      => __('Summarization', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
            'analysis'          => __('Analysis', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        ];

        return isset($types[$type]) ? $types[$type] : esc_html($type);
    }

    /**
     * Get status HTML.
     */
    private function get_status_html($status) {
        $statuses = [
            'pending'   => ['label' => __('Pending', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-pending'],
            'running'   => ['label' => __('Running', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-running'],
            'completed' => ['label' => __('Completed', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-completed'],
            'failed'    => ['label' => __('Failed', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-failed'],
            'cancelled' => ['label' => __('Cancelled', 'ai-magic-publisher'), 'class' => 'status-cancelled']
        ];

        return isset($statuses[$status]) ? sprintf(
            '<span class="%s">%s</span>',
            esc_attr($statuses[$status]['class']),
            esc_html($statuses[$status]['label'])
        ) : esc_html($status);
    }
}

/**
 * AI Magic Publisher Admin JavaScript
 * Version: 1.0.0
 * Current User: aimastera069
 * Last Updated: 2025-03-26 18:37:55 UTC
 */

(function($) {
    'use strict';

    // Main admin class
    class AIMagicAdmin {
        constructor() {
            this.currentUser = 'aimastera069';
            this.lastUpdate = '2025-03-26 18:37:55';
            
            this.initializeComponents();
            this.setupEventListeners();
            this.initializePolling();
        }

        initializeComponents() {
            this.taskManager = new TaskManager();
            this.userManager = new UserManager();
            this.tenantManager = new TenantManager();
            this.settingsManager = new SettingsManager();
            this.uiComponents = new UIComponents();
        }

        setupEventListeners() {
            // Global event listeners
            $(document).on('aimagic:taskUpdated', this.handleTaskUpdate.bind(this));
            $(document).on('aimagic:userUpdated', this.handleUserUpdate.bind(this));
            $(document).on('aimagic:tenantUpdated', this.handleTenantUpdate.bind(this));
            
            // Error handling
            window.onerror = this.handleGlobalError.bind(this);
        }

        initializePolling() {
            // Poll for updates every 30 seconds
            setInterval(() => {
                this.taskManager.pollForUpdates();
            }, 30000);
        }

        handleGlobalError(msg, url, line, col, error) {
            this.uiComponents.showToast({
                message: 'An error occurred: ' + msg,
                type: 'error',
                duration: 5000
            });
            console.error('AI Magic Publisher Error:', { msg, url, line, col, error });
        }

        handleTaskUpdate(event, data) {
            this.uiComponents.updateDashboardStats();
            this.taskManager.refreshTaskList();
        }

        handleUserUpdate(event, data) {
            this.uiComponents.updateDashboardStats();
            this.userManager.refreshUserList();
        }

        handleTenantUpdate(event, data) {
            this.uiComponents.updateDashboardStats();
            this.tenantManager.refreshTenantList();
        }
    }

    // Task Management
    class TaskManager {
        constructor() {
            this.initializeTaskComponents();
        }

        initializeTaskComponents() {
            // Task list functionality
            $('.aimagic-task-list').each((index, element) => {
                this.initializeTaskList($(element));
            });

            // Task actions
            $('.retry-task').on('click', this.handleTaskRetry.bind(this));
            $('.delete-task').on('click', this.handleTaskDelete.bind(this));
            $('.view-task-details').on('click', this.handleTaskView.bind(this));
        }

        async handleTaskRetry(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            const taskId = $(event.currentTarget).data('task-id');
            
            try {
                await this.retryTask(taskId);
                this.refreshTaskList();
                UIComponents.showToast({
                    message: 'Task retry initiated successfully',
                    type: 'success'
                });
            } catch (error) {
                UIComponents.showToast({
                    message: 'Failed to retry task: ' + error.message,
                    type: 'error'
                });
            }
        }

        async retryTask(taskId) {
            const response = await $.ajax({
                url: ajaxurl,
                method: 'POST',
                data: {
                    action: 'aimagic_retry_task',
                    task_id: taskId,
                    nonce: aimagic_data.nonce
                }
            });

            if (!response.success) {
                throw new Error(response.data.message);
            }

            return response.data;
        }

        pollForUpdates() {
            $.ajax({
                url: ajaxurl,
                method: 'GET',
                data: {
                    action: 'aimagic_get_task_updates',
                    last_update: this.lastUpdate,
                    nonce: aimagic_data.nonce
                },
                success: (response) => {
                    if (response.success && response.data.updates) {
                        this.handleTaskUpdates(response.data.updates);
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        handleTaskUpdates(updates) {
            updates.forEach(update => {
                $(document).trigger('aimagic:taskUpdated', [update]);
                this.updateTaskInList(update);
            });
        }

        updateTaskInList(taskData) {
            const $row = $(`#task-${taskData.id}`);
            if ($row.length) {
                $row.find('.column-status').html(this.getStatusBadgeHtml(taskData.status));
                $row.find('.column-updated_at').text(taskData.updated_at);
            }
        }

        getStatusBadgeHtml(status) {
            const statusClasses = {
                pending: 'status-pending',
                processing: 'status-processing',
                completed: 'status-completed',
                failed: 'status-failed'
            };

            return `<span class="status-badge ${statusClasses[status] || ''}">${status}</span>`;
        }
    }

    // User Management
    class UserManager {
        constructor() {
            this.initializeUserComponents();
        }

        initializeUserComponents() {
            $('.reset-quota').on('click', this.handleQuotaReset.bind(this));
            $('.delete-user').on('click', this.handleUserDelete.bind(this));
            $('#add-new-user').on('click', this.handleNewUser.bind(this));
        }

        async handleQuotaReset(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            const userId = $(event.currentTarget).data('user-id');

            if (!confirm('Are you sure you want to reset this user\'s quota?')) {
                return;
            }

            try {
                await this.resetUserQuota(userId);
                UIComponents.showToast({
                    message: 'User quota reset successfully',
                    type: 'success'
                });
                this.refreshUserList();
            } catch (error) {
                UIComponents.showToast({
                    message: 'Failed to reset quota: ' + error.message,
                    type: 'error'
                });
            }
        }

        async resetUserQuota(userId) {
            const response = await $.ajax({
                url: ajaxurl,
                method: 'POST',
                data: {
                    action: 'aimagic_reset_user_quota',
                    user_id: userId,
                    nonce: aimagic_data.nonce
                }
            });

            if (!response.success) {
                throw new Error(response.data.message);
            }

            return response.data;
        }
    }

    // Tenant Management
    class TenantManager {
        constructor() {
            this.initializeTenantComponents();
        }

        initializeTenantComponents() {
            $('.toggle-tenant-status').on('click', this.handleStatusToggle.bind(this));
            $('.copy-api-key').on('click', this.handleApiKeyCopy.bind(this));
            $('#add-new-tenant').on('click', this.handleNewTenant.bind(this));
        }

        async handleStatusToggle(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            const tenantId = $(event.currentTarget).data('tenant-id');
            const newStatus = $(event.currentTarget).data('new-status');

            try {
                await this.updateTenantStatus(tenantId, newStatus);
                UIComponents.showToast({
                    message: 'Tenant status updated successfully',
                    type: 'success'
                });
                this.refreshTenantList();
            } catch (error) {
                UIComponents.showToast({
                    message: 'Failed to update status: ' + error.message,
                    type: 'error'
                });
            }
        }

        async handleApiKeyCopy(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            const apiKey = $(event.currentTarget).data('api-key');
            
            try {
                await navigator.clipboard.writeText(apiKey);
                UIComponents.showToast({
                    message: 'API key copied to clipboard',
                    type: 'success'
                });
            } catch (error) {
                UIComponents.showToast({
                    message: 'Failed to copy API key',
                    type: 'error'
                });
            }
        }
    }

    // Settings Management
    class SettingsManager {
        constructor() {
            this.initializeSettingsComponents();
        }

        initializeSettingsComponents() {
            this.setupApiKeyValidation();
            this.setupWebhookUrlCopy();
            this.setupSettingsValidation();
        }

        setupApiKeyValidation() {
            $('#aimagic_gpt4_api_key').on('change', async (event) => {
                const apiKey = $(event.currentTarget).val();
                if (apiKey) {
                    await this.validateApiKey(apiKey);
                }
            });
        }

        async validateApiKey(apiKey) {
            try {
                const response = await $.ajax({
                    url: ajaxurl,
                    method: 'POST',
                    data: {
                        action: 'aimagic_validate_api_key',
                        api_key: apiKey,
                        nonce: aimagic_data.nonce
                    }
                });

                if (response.success) {
                    UIComponents.showToast({
                        message: 'API key validated successfully',
                        type: 'success'
                    });
                } else {
                    UIComponents.showToast({
                        message: 'Invalid API key',
                        type: 'error'
                    });
                }
            } catch (error) {
                UIComponents.showToast({
                    message: 'Failed to validate API key',
                    type: 'error'
                });
            }
        }
    }

    // UI Components
    class UIComponents {
        static showToast({ message, type = 'info', duration = 3000 }) {
            const toast = $(`
                <div class="aimagic-toast aimagic-toast-${type}">
                    ${message}
                </div>
            `).appendTo('body');

            setTimeout(() => {
                toast.fadeOut(300, function() {
                    $(this).remove();
                });
            }, duration);
        }

        static showModal(content) {
            const modal = $(`
                <div class="task-details-modal-backdrop"></div>
                <div class="task-details-modal">
                    <div class="modal-header">
                        <h2>${content.title}</h2>
                        <button class="close-modal">&times;</button>
                    </div>
                    <div class="modal-content">
                        ${content.body}
                    </div>
                    <div class="modal-footer">
                        ${content.footer || ''}
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).appendTo('body');

            $('.close-modal').on('click', () => {
                modal.fadeOut(300, function() {
                    $(this).remove();
                });
            });
        }

        updateDashboardStats() {
            $.ajax({
                url: ajaxurl,
                method: 'GET',
                data: {
                    action: 'aimagic_get_dashboard_stats',
                    nonce: aimagic_data.nonce
                },
                success: (response) => {
                    if (response.success) {
                        this.renderDashboardStats(response.data);
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        renderDashboardStats(stats) {
            Object.entries(stats).forEach(([key, value]) => {
                $(`#stat-${key}`).text(value);
            });
        }
    }

    // Initialize admin functionality when document is ready
    $(document).ready(() => {
        window.aimagicAdmin = new AIMagicAdmin();
    });

})(jQuery);

目錄：/www/wwwroot/xart004.heatgroups.top/wp-content/plugins/ai_plateform_v2/files_2025/includes
檔名：class-notification.php
==================================================
<?php
namespace AIMagic;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

class Notification {
    private $settings;
    private $logger;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->settings = get_option('aimagic_settings', []);
        $this->logger = new Logger();

        add_action('aimagic_task_completed', [$this, 'notify_task_completion'], 10, 2);
        add_action('aimagic_quota_exceeded', [$this, 'notify_quota_exceeded'], 10, 2);
    }

    /**
     * Send notification
     */
    public function send($type, $data, $recipients = []) {
        $methods = $this->get_notification_methods();

        foreach ($methods as $method) {
            try {
                $this->send_via_method($method, $type, $data, $recipients);
            } catch (\Exception $e) {
                $this->logger->error('Notification failed', [
                    'method' => $method,
                    'type' => $type,
                    'error' => $e->getMessage()
                ]);
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send notification via specific method
     */
    private function send_via_method($method, $type, $data, $recipients) {
        switch ($method) {
            case 'email':
                $this->send_email($type, $data, $recipients);
                break;
            case 'webhook':
                $this->send_webhook($type, $data);
                break;
            case 'line':
                $this->send_line($type, $data, $recipients);
                break;
            case 'wechat':
                $this->send_wechat($type, $data, $recipients);
                break;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send email notification
     */
    private function send_email($type, $data, $recipients) {
        if (empty($recipients)) {
            $recipients = [$this->settings['monitoring']['notify_email']];
        }

        $subject = $this->get_email_subject($type, $data);
        $message = $this->get_email_message($type, $data);
        $headers = ['Content-Type: text/html; charset=UTF-8'];

        foreach ($recipients as $recipient) {
            wp_mail($recipient, $subject, $message, $headers);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send webhook notification
     */
    private function send_webhook($type, $data) {
        $webhook_url = $this->get_webhook_url($type);
        if (!$webhook_url) {
            return;
        }

        $response = wp_remote_post($webhook_url, [
            'headers' => [
                'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
                'X-AImagic-Event' => $type,
                'X-AImagic-Signature' => $this->generate_signature($data)
            ],
            'body' => json_encode($data),
            'timeout' => $this->settings['webhooks']['timeout'] ?? 5
        ]);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            throw new \Exception($response->get_error_message());
        }

        $status_code = wp_remote_retrieve_response_code($response);
        if ($status_code < 200 || $status_code >= 300) {
            throw new \Exception("Webhook failed with status: $status_code");
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send LINE notification
     */
    private function send_line($type, $data, $recipients) {
        $line = new \AIMagic\Integrations\LINEIntegration();
        $message = $this->get_line_message($type, $data);

        foreach ($recipients as $recipient) {
            $line->send_message($recipient, $message);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Send WeChat notification
     */
    private function send_wechat($type, $data, $recipients) {
        $wechat = new \AIMagic\Integrations\WeChatIntegration();
        $message = $this->get_wechat_message($type, $data);

        foreach ($recipients as $recipient) {
            $wechat->send_message($recipient, $message);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Handle task completion notification
     */
    public function notify_task_completion($task_id, $result) {
        global $wpdb;
        $task = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT t.*, u.user_id, tn.name as tenant_name
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks t
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_users u ON t.user_id = u.id
            LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants tn ON t.tenant_id = tn.id
            WHERE t.id = %d",
            $task_id
        ));

        if (!$task) return;

        $user = get_userdata($task->user_id);
        if (!$user) return;

        $data = [
            'task_id' => $task_id,
            'type' => $task->type,
            'status' => $result['status'],
            'tenant' => $task->tenant_name,
            'user' => $user->display_name,
            'completed_at' => current_time('mysql')
        ];

        $this->send('task_completed', $data, [$user->user_email]);
    }

    /**
     * Handle quota exceeded notification
     */
    public function notify_quota_exceeded($tenant_id, $usage_data) {
        global $wpdb;
        $tenant = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants WHERE id = %d",
            $tenant_id
        ));

        if (!$tenant) return;

        $admin_email = $this->settings['monitoring']['notify_email'];
        $data = [
            'tenant_id' => $tenant_id,
            'tenant_name' => $tenant->name,
            'quota_used' => $usage_data['used'],
            'quota_limit' => $usage_data['limit'],
            'percentage' => $usage_data['percentage']
        ];

        $this->send('quota_exceeded', $data, [$admin_email]);
    }

    /**
     * Get notification methods
     */
    private function get_notification_methods() {
        $methods = ['email'];

        if (!empty($this->settings['webhooks']['success_url'])) {
            $methods[] = 'webhook';
        }

        if (!empty($this->settings['line']['channel_token'])) {
            $methods[] = 'line';
        }

        if (!empty($this->settings['wechat']['app_id'])) {
            $methods[] = 'wechat';
        }

        return $methods;
    }

    /**
     * Get webhook URL for notification type
     */
    private function get_webhook_url($type) {
        switch ($type) {
            case 'task_completed':
                return $this->settings['webhooks']['success_url'];
            case 'error':
                return $this->settings['webhooks']['error_url'];
            default:
                return '';
        }
    }

    /**
     * Generate webhook signature
     */
    private function generate_signature($data) {
        $secret = $this->settings['webhooks']['secret'] ?? '';
        return hash_hmac('sha256', json_encode($data), $secret);
    }

    /**
     * Get email subject
     */
    private function get_email_subject($type, $data) {
        $site_name = get_bloginfo('name');

        switch ($type) {
            case 'task_completed':
                return sprintf(
                    __('[%s] Task #%d Completed', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    $site_name,
                    $data['task_id']
                );
            case 'quota_exceeded':
                return sprintf(
                    __('[%s] Quota Exceeded Alert - %s', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    $site_name,
                    $data['tenant_name']
                );
            default:
                return sprintf(
                    __('[%s] Notification', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    $site_name
                );
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get email message
     */
    private function get_email_message($type, $data) {
        ob_start();
        include(AIMAGIC_PLUGIN_DIR . 'templates/emails/' . $type . '.php');
        return ob_get_clean();
    }

    /**
     * Get LINE message
     */
    private function get_line_message($type, $data) {
        switch ($type) {
            case 'task_completed':
                return [
                    'type' => 'text',
                    'text' => sprintf(
                        __("Task #%d has been completed.\nType: %s\nStatus: %s", 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                        $data['task_id'],
                        $data['type'],
                        $data['status']
                    )
                ];
            case 'quota_exceeded':
                return [
                    'type' => 'text',
                    'text' => sprintf(
                        __("Quota exceeded alert!\nTenant: %s\nUsage: %s / %s", 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                        $data['tenant_name'],
                        size_format($data['quota_used']),
                        size_format($data['quota_limit'])
                    )
                ];
            default:
                return [
                    'type' => 'text',
                    'text' => json_encode($data)
                ];
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get WeChat message
     */
    private function get_wechat_message($type, $data) {
        // Similar to LINE messages but formatted for WeChat
        return $this->get_line_message($type, $data)['text'];
    }
}

目錄：/www/wwwroot/xart004.heatgroups.top/wp-content/plugins/ai_plateform_v2/files_2025/includes
檔名：class-api-handler.php
==================================================
<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class APIHandler {
    private $rate_limiter;
    private $validator;
    private $logger;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->rate_limiter = new RateLimiter();
        $this->validator = new RequestValidator();
        $this->logger = new Logger();
    }

    public function handle_request($endpoint, $method = 'GET') {
        try {
            // Verify API key
            $api_key = $this->get_api_key();
            if (!Security::verify_api_key($api_key)) {
                throw new \Exception('Invalid API key', 401);
            }

            // Check rate limit
            if (!$this->rate_limiter->check($api_key)) {
                throw new \Exception('Rate limit exceeded', 429);
            }

            // Validate request method
            if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] !== $method) {
                throw new \Exception('Method not allowed', 405);
            }

            // Handle specific endpoints
            switch ($endpoint) {
                case 'tasks':
                    return $this->handle_tasks_endpoint($method);
                
                case 'webhooks':
                    return $this->handle_webhooks_endpoint($method);
                
                case 'quotas':
                    return $this->handle_quotas_endpoint($method);
                
                default:
                    throw new \Exception('Endpoint not found', 404);
            }
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $this->logger->error('API Error: ' . $e->getMessage(), [
                'endpoint' => $endpoint,
                'method' => $method,
                'code' => $e->getCode()
            ]);

            return $this->send_error_response(
                $e->getMessage(),
                $e->getCode() ?: 500
            );
        }
    }

    private function handle_tasks_endpoint($method) {
        switch ($method) {
            case 'GET':
                $rules = [
                    'page' => ['type' => 'int', 'min' => 1],
                    'per_page' => ['type' => 'int', 'min' => 1, 'max' => 100],
                    'status' => ['in' => ['pending', 'running', 'completed', 'failed']],
                    'type' => ['in' => ['content_generation', 'image_generation', 'translation']]
                ];

                if (!$this->validator->validate_request($rules)) {
                    return $this->send_error_response(
                        $this->validator->get_first_error(),
                        400
                    );
                }

                return $this->get_tasks();

            case 'POST':
                $rules = [
                    'type' => ['required' => true, 'in' => ['content_generation', 'image_generation', 'translation']],
                    'content' => ['required' => true, 'type' => 'string', 'min' => 1],
                    'priority' => ['in' => ['normal', 'high', 'urgent']]
                ];

                if (!$this->validator->validate_request($rules)) {
                    return $this->send_error_response(
                        $this->validator->get_first_error(),
                        400
                    );
                }

                return $this->create_task();

            default:
                throw new \Exception('Method not allowed', 405);
        }
    }

    private function get_api_key() {
        $headers = getallheaders();
        
        // Check Authorization header
        if (isset($headers['Authorization'])) {
            if (preg_match('/^Bearer\s+(.*)$/i', $headers['Authorization'], $matches)) {
                return $matches[1];
            }
        }

        // Check query parameter
        return $_GET['api_key'] ?? null;
    }

    private function send_error_response($message, $code) {
        http_response_code($code);
        return wp_send_json([
            'success' => false,
            'error' => $message,
            'code' => $code
        ]);
    }

    private function send_success_response($data) {
        return wp_send_json([
            'success' => true,
            'data' => $data
        ]);
    }
}

class Settings {

    public function __construct() {

    /**

    /**
     * Sanitize settings
     */
    public function sanitize_settings($input) {
        $sanitized = [];

        // API Keys
        $sanitized['api_keys'] = [
            'openai' => sanitize_text_field($input['api_keys']['openai'] ?? ''),
            'line' => sanitize_text_field($input['api_keys']['line'] ?? ''),
            'wechat' => sanitize_text_field($input['api_keys']['wechat'] ?? '')
        ];

        // Endpoints
        $sanitized['endpoints'] = [
            'openai' => esc_url_raw($input['endpoints']['openai'] ?? $this->defaults['endpoints']['openai']),
            'line' => esc_url_raw($input['endpoints']['line'] ?? $this->defaults['endpoints']['line']),
            'wechat' => esc_url_raw($input['endpoints']['wechat'] ?? $this->defaults['endpoints']['wechat'])
        ];

        // Defaults
        $sanitized['defaults'] = [
            'model' => sanitize_text_field($input['defaults']['model'] ?? $this->defaults['defaults']['model']),
            'temperature' => floatval($input['defaults']['temperature'] ?? $this->defaults['defaults']['temperature']),
            'max_tokens' => intval($input['defaults']['max_tokens'] ?? $this->defaults['defaults']['max_tokens'])
        ];

        // Limits
        $sanitized['limits'] = [
            'max_tokens' => intval($input['limits']['max_tokens'] ?? $this->defaults['limits']['max_tokens']),
            'max_requests_per_minute' => intval($input['limits']['max_requests_per_minute'] ?? $this->defaults['limits']['max_requests_per_minute']),
            'max_concurrent_tasks' => intval($input['limits']['max_concurrent_tasks'] ?? $this->defaults['limits']['max_concurrent_tasks'])
        ];

        // Cache
        $sanitized['cache'] = [
            'enable_cache' => (bool) ($input['cache']['enable_cache'] ?? $this->defaults['cache']['enable_cache']),
            'cache_duration' => intval($input['cache']['cache_duration'] ?? $this->defaults['cache']['cache_duration']),
            'max_cache_size' => intval($input['cache']['max_cache_size'] ?? $this->defaults['cache']['max_cache_size'])
        ];

        // Monitoring
        $sanitized['monitoring'] = [
            'enable_logging' => (bool) ($input['monitoring']['enable_logging'] ?? $this->defaults['monitoring']['enable_logging']),
            'log_retention' => intval($input['monitoring']['log_retention'] ?? $this->defaults['monitoring']['log_retention']),
            'alert_threshold' => intval($input['monitoring']['alert_threshold'] ?? $this->defaults['monitoring']['alert_threshold']),
            'notify_email' => sanitize_email($input['monitoring']['notify_email'] ?? $this->defaults['monitoring']['notify_email'])
        ];

        // Webhooks
        $sanitized['webhooks'] = [
            'success_url' => esc_url_raw($input['webhooks']['success_url'] ?? ''),
            'error_url' => esc_url_raw($input['webhooks']['error_url'] ?? ''),
            'secret' => sanitize_text_field($input['webhooks']['secret'] ?? $this->defaults['webhooks']['secret']),
            'timeout' => intval($input['webhooks']['timeout'] ?? $this->defaults['webhooks']['timeout']),
            'retry_attempts' => intval($input['webhooks']['retry_attempts'] ?? $this->defaults['webhooks']['retry_attempts'])
        ];

        // Optimization
        $sanitized['optimization'] = [
            'batch_size' => intval($input['optimization']['batch_size'] ?? $this->defaults['optimization']['batch_size']),
            'parallel_requests' => intval($input['optimization']['parallel_requests'] ?? $this->defaults['optimization']['parallel_requests']),
            'retry_attempts' => intval($input['optimization']['retry_attempts'] ?? $this->defaults['optimization']['retry_attempts'])
        ];

        return $sanitized;
    }

    /**
     * Render section headers
     */
    public function render_api_section() {
        echo '<p>' . __('Configure your API keys and endpoints.', 'ai-magic-publisher') . '</p>';
    }

    public function render_model_section() {
        echo '<p>' . __('Configure AI model settings.', 'ai-magic-publisher') . '</p>';
    }

    public function render_cache_section() {
        echo '<p>' . __('Configure caching settings.', 'ai-magic-publisher') . '</p>';
    }

    public function render_monitoring_section() {
        echo '<p>' . __('Configure monitoring and logging settings.', 'ai-magic-publisher') . '</p>';
    }

    public function render_webhook_section() {
        echo '<p>' . __('Configure webhook notifications.', 'ai-magic-publisher') . '</p>';
    }

    /**
     * Render form fields
     */
    public function render_text_field($args) {
        $id = $args['id'];
        $value = $this->get_setting_value($id);
        $type = isset($args['password']) ? 'password' : 'text';
        
        printf(
            '<input type="%s" id="%s" name="aimagic_settings[%s]" value="%s" class="regular-text">',
            $type,
            esc_attr($id),
            esc_attr($id),
            esc_attr($value)
        );

        if (!empty($args['description'])) {
            printf('<p class="description">%s</p>', esc_html($args['description']));
        }
    }

    public function render_select_field($args) {
        $id = $args['id'];
        $value = $this->get_setting_value($id);
        $options = $args['options'];

        printf('<select id="%s" name="aimagic_settings[%s]">', esc_attr($id), esc_attr($id));
        
        foreach ($options as $key => $label) {
            printf(
                '<option value="%s" %s>%s</option>',
                esc_attr($key),
                selected($value, $key, false),
                esc_html($label)
            );
        }

        echo '</select>';

        if (!empty($args['description'])) {
            printf('<p class="description">%s</p>', esc_html($args['description']));
        }
    }

    public function render_checkbox_field($args) {
        $id = $args['id'];
        $value = $this->get_setting_value($id);

        printf(
            '<input type="checkbox" id="%s" name="aimagic_settings[%s]" value="1" %s>',
            esc_attr($id),
            esc_attr($id),
            checked($value, true, false)
        );

        if (!empty($args['description'])) {
            printf('<p class="description">%s</p>', esc_html($args['description']));
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get setting value
     */
    private function get_setting_value($key) {
        $parts = explode('[', str_replace(']', '', $key));
        $value = $this->settings;

        foreach ($parts as $part) {
            if (!isset($value[$part])) {
                $value = $this->get_default_value($parts);
                break;
            }
            $value = $value[$part];
        }

        return $value;
    }

    /**
     * Get default value
     */
    private function get_default_value($parts) {
        $value = $this->defaults;

        foreach ($parts as $part) {
            if (!isset($value[$part])) {
                return '';
            }
            $value = $value[$part];
        }

        return $value;
    }
}

目錄：/www/wwwroot/xart004.heatgroups.top/wp-content/plugins/ai_plateform_v2/files_2025/includes/Admin
檔名：class-admin-nodes-list.php

<?php
namespace AIMagic\Admin;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

if (!class_exists('WP_List_Table')) {
    require_once(ABSPATH . 'wp-admin/includes/class-wp-list-table.php');
}

class Nodes_List_Table extends \WP_List_Table {
    public function __construct() {
        parent::__construct([
            'singular' => 'node',
            'plural'   => 'nodes',
            'ajax'     => true
        ]);
    }

    public function get_columns() {
        return [
            'cb'              => '<input type="checkbox" />',
            'node_id'         => __('Node ID', 'aimagic'),
            'node_type'       => __('Type', 'aimagic'),
            'status'          => __('Status', 'aimagic'),
            'last_heartbeat'  => __('Last Heartbeat', 'aimagic'),
            'tasks_completed' => __('Tasks Completed', 'aimagic'),
            'avg_processing'  => __('Avg. Processing Time', 'aimagic'),
            'registered_at'   => __('Registered', 'aimagic'),
            'actions'         => __('Actions', 'aimagic')
        ];
    }

    public function prepare_items() {
        global $wpdb;

        $per_page = 20;
        $current_page = $this->get_pagenum();
        $total_items = $wpdb->get_var("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {$wpdb->prefix}ai_nodes");

        $this->set_pagination_args([
            'total_items' => $total_items,
            'per_page'    => $per_page
        ]);

        $this->items = $wpdb->get_results($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT n.*, 
                    COUNT(t.id) as tasks_completed,
                    AVG(t.processing_time) as avg_processing_time
             FROM {$wpdb->prefix}ai_nodes n
             LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->prefix}ai_tasks t ON n.node_id = t.node_id
             GROUP BY n.node_id
             ORDER BY n.registered_at DESC
             LIMIT %d OFFSET %d",
            $per_page,
            ($current_page - 1) * $per_page
        ));
    }

    public function column_default($item, $column_name) {
        switch ($column_name) {
            case 'node_id':
                return '#' . $item->node_id;
            case 'node_type':
                return $this->get_node_type_label($item->node_type);
            case 'status':
                return $this->get_status_html($item);
            case 'last_heartbeat':
                return $this->format_heartbeat_time($item->last_heartbeat);
            case 'tasks_completed':
                return number_format($item->tasks_completed);
            case 'avg_processing':
                return $item->avg_processing_time ? 
                    round($item->avg_processing_time, 2) . 's' : 
                    '-';
            case 'registered_at':
                return wp_date('Y-m-d H:i:s', strtotime($item->registered_at));
            case 'actions':
                return $this->get_row_actions($item);
            default:
                return print_r($item, true);
        }
    }

    private function get_node_type_label($type) {
        $labels = [
            'text_node'  => '<span class="node-type text">Text</span>',
            'image_node' => '<span class="node-type image">Image</span>',
            'video_node' => '<span class="node-type video">Video</span>'
        ];
        return isset($labels[$type]) ? $labels[$type] : ucfirst($type);
    }

    private function get_status_html($item) {
        $current_time = current_time('timestamp');
        $last_heartbeat = strtotime($item->last_heartbeat);
        $diff = $current_time - $last_heartbeat;

        if ($diff > 300) { // 5 minutes
            return '<span class="status-offline">Offline</span>';
        } elseif ($diff > 60) { // 1 minute
            return '<span class="status-warning">Warning</span>';
        } else {
            return '<span class="status-active">Active</span>';
        }
    }

    private function format_heartbeat_time($timestamp) {
        $current_time = current_time('timestamp');
        $heartbeat_time = strtotime($timestamp);
        $diff = $current_time - $heartbeat_time;

        if ($diff < 60) {
            return sprintf(_n('%s second ago', '%s seconds ago', $diff, 'aimagic'), $diff);
        } elseif ($diff < 3600) {
            $minutes = floor($diff / 60);
            return sprintf(_n('%s minute ago', '%s minutes ago', $minutes, 'aimagic'), $minutes);
        } else {
            return wp_date('Y-m-d H:i:s', $heartbeat_time);
        }
    }

    private function get_row_actions($item) {
        $actions = [
            'view' => sprintf(
                '<a href="%s">View</a>',
                admin_url('admin.php?page=aimagic-nodes&action=view&id=' . $item->node_id)
            ),
            'edit' => sprintf(
                '<a href="%s">Edit</a>',
                admin_url('admin.php?page=aimagic-nodes&action=edit&id=' . $item->node_id)
            )
        ];

        if ($this->is_node_offline($item)) {
            $actions['delete'] = sprintf(
                '<a href="%s" class="delete" onclick="return confirm(\'%s\');">Delete</a>',
                wp_nonce_url(admin_url('admin.php?page=aimagic-nodes&action=delete&id=' . $item->node_id), 'delete_node_' . $item->node_id),
                __('Are you sure you want to delete this node?', 'aimagic')
            );
        }

        return $this->row_actions($actions);
    }

    private function is_node_offline($item) {
        $current_time = current_time('timestamp');
        $last_heartbeat = strtotime($item->last_heartbeat);
        return ($current_time - $last_heartbeat) > 300;
    }

    public function column_cb($item) {
        return sprintf(
            '<input type="checkbox" name="nodes[]" value="%s" />',
            $item->node_id
        );
    }

    public function get_bulk_actions() {
        return [
            'delete' => __('Delete', 'aimagic')
        ];
    }

    public function process_bulk_action() {
        if ('delete' === $this->current_action()) {
            $nonce = esc_attr($_REQUEST['_wpnonce']);
            if (!wp_verify_nonce($nonce, 'bulk-' . $this->_args['plural'])) {
                die('Security check failed');
            }

            global $wpdb;
            $nodes = isset($_REQUEST['nodes']) ? array_map('intval', $_REQUEST['nodes']) : array();
            
            if (!empty($nodes)) {
                foreach ($nodes as $node_id) {
                    // Only delete offline nodes
                    $node = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
                        "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}ai_nodes WHERE node_id = %d",
                        $node_id
                    ));

                    if ($node && $this->is_node_offline($node)) {
                        $wpdb->delete(
                            $wpdb->prefix . 'ai_nodes',
                            ['node_id' => $node_id],
                            ['%d']
                        );
                    }
                }
                
                wp_redirect(add_query_arg('message', '3', wp_get_referer()));
                exit;
            }
        }
    }
}
