<?php
namespace AIMagic\Core;

class NodeManager {
    private static $instance = null;
    private $error_handler;
    
    private function __construct() {
        $this->error_handler = ErrorHandler::getInstance();
        
        // Schedule node cleanup
        if (!wp_next_scheduled('aimagic_cleanup_nodes')) {
            wp_schedule_event(time(), 'fifteen_minutes', 'aimagic_cleanup_nodes');
        }
        add_action('aimagic_cleanup_nodes', array($this, 'cleanup_offline_nodes'));
    }

    public static function instance() {
        if (self::$instance === null) {
            self::$instance = new self();
        }
        return self::$instance;
    }

    public function register_node($node_type) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        try {
            $auth_token = wp_generate_password(32, false);
            
            $wpdb->insert(
                $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_nodes',
                array(
                    'node_type' => $node_type,
                    'auth_token' => $auth_token,
                    'status' => 'active',
                    'last_heartbeat' => current_time('mysql'),
                    'registered_at' => current_time('mysql')
                ),
                array('%s', '%s', '%s', '%s', '%s')
            );
            
            return array(
                'node_id' => $wpdb->insert_id,
                'auth_token' => $auth_token
            );
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $this->error_handler->log_error($e, array(
                'component' => 'node_manager',
                'operation' => 'register_node',
                'node_type' => $node_type
            ));
            return false;
        }
    }

    public function update_heartbeat($node_id) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        try {
            return $wpdb->update(
                $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_nodes',
                array('last_heartbeat' => current_time('mysql')),
                array('id' => $node_id),
                array('%s'),
                array('%d')
            );
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $this->error_handler->log_error($e, array(
                'component' => 'node_manager',
                'operation' => 'update_heartbeat',
                'node_id' => $node_id
            ));
            return false;
        }
    }

    public function get_available_nodes($node_type = null) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        $sql = "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_nodes 
                WHERE status = 'active' 
                AND last_heartbeat > DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 10 MINUTE)";
                
        if ($node_type) {
            $sql .= $wpdb->prepare(" AND node_type = %s", $node_type);
        }
        
        try {
            return $wpdb->get_results($sql);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $this->error_handler->log_error($e, array(
                'component' => 'node_manager',
                'operation' => 'get_available_nodes',
                'node_type' => $node_type
            ));
            return array();
        }
    }

    public function cleanup_offline_nodes() {
        global $wpdb;
        
        try {
            return $wpdb->query(
                "UPDATE {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_nodes 
                 SET status = 'offline' 
                 WHERE last_heartbeat < DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 10 MINUTE)"
            );
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $this->error_handler->log_error($e, array(
                'component' => 'node_manager',
                'operation' => 'cleanup_offline_nodes'
            ));
            return false;
        }
    }

    public function validate_node($node_id, $auth_token) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        try {
            $node = $wpdb->get_row(
                $wpdb->prepare(
                    "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_nodes 
                     WHERE id = %d AND auth_token = %s AND status = 'active'",
                    $node_id,
                    $auth_token
                )
            );
            
            return $node !== null;
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $this->error_handler->log_error($e, array(
                'component' => 'node_manager',
                'operation' => 'validate_node',
                'node_id' => $node_id
            ));
            return false;
        }
    }

    public function get_node_stats($node_type = null) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        $conditions = array("1=1");
        if ($node_type) {
            $conditions[] = $wpdb->prepare("node_type = %s", $node_type);
        }
        
        $where = implode(" AND ", $conditions);
        
        try {
            return array(
                'total' => $wpdb->get_var("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_nodes WHERE $where"),
                'active' => $wpdb->get_var("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_nodes WHERE $where AND status = 'active'"),
                'offline' => $wpdb->get_var("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_nodes WHERE $where AND status = 'offline'")
            );
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $this->error_handler->log_error($e, array(
                'component' => 'node_manager',
                'operation' => 'get_node_stats',
                'node_type' => $node_type
            ));
            return array(
                'total' => 0,
                'active' => 0,
                'offline' => 0
            );
        }
    }
}

檔名：class-optimizer.php
==================================================
<?php
namespace AIMagic;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

class Optimizer {
    private $settings;
    private $batch_size;
    private $parallel_requests;
    private $retry_attempts;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->settings = get_option('aimagic_settings', []);
        $this->batch_size = $this->settings['optimization']['batch_size'] ?? 10;
        $this->parallel_requests = $this->settings['optimization']['parallel_requests'] ?? 5;
        $this->retry_attempts = $this->settings['optimization']['retry_attempts'] ?? 3;
    }

    /**
     * Process items in batches
     */
    public function process_in_batches($items, $callback) {
        $total = count($items);
        $processed = 0;
        $results = [];

        while ($processed < $total) {
            $batch = array_slice($items, $processed, $this->batch_size);
            $batch_results = $this->process_batch($batch, $callback);
            $results = array_merge($results, $batch_results);
            $processed += count($batch);

            if ($processed < $total) {
                $this->maybe_pause();
            }
        }

        return $results;
    }

    /**
     * Process batch of items
     */
    private function process_batch($items, $callback) {
        $results = [];
        $chunks = array_chunk($items, $this->parallel_requests);

        foreach ($chunks as $chunk) {
            $promises = [];
            
            foreach ($chunk as $item) {
                $promises[] = $this->process_with_retry($item, $callback);
            }

            $chunk_results = array_filter($promises);
            $results = array_merge($results, $chunk_results);
        }

        return $results;
    }

    /**
     * Process item with retry logic
     */
    private function process_with_retry($item, $callback) {
        $attempts = 0;
        $result = null;
        $last_error = null;

        while ($attempts < $this->retry_attempts) {
            try {
                $result = $callback($item);
                break;
            } catch (\Exception $e) {
                $last_error = $e;
                $attempts++;
                
                if ($attempts < $this->retry_attempts) {
                    $this->exponential_backoff($attempts);
                }
            }
        }

        if ($result === null && $last_error) {
            throw $last_error;
        }

        return $result;
    }

    /**
     * Exponential backoff delay
     */
    private function exponential_backoff($attempt) {
        $delay = min(pow(2, $attempt) * 100, 1000);
        usleep($delay * 1000);
    }

    /**
     * Pause processing if needed
     */
    private function maybe_pause() {
        if ($this->memory_exceeded() || $this->time_exceeded()) {
            sleep(1);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Check if memory limit exceeded
     */
    private function memory_exceeded() {
        $memory_limit = $this->get_memory_limit() * 0.9;
        $current_memory = memory_get_usage(true);
        return $current_memory >= $memory_limit;
    }

    /**
     * Get memory limit in bytes
     */
    private function get_memory_limit() {
        if (function_exists('ini_get')) {
            $memory_limit = ini_get('memory_limit');
        } else {
            $memory_limit = '128M';
        }

        if (!$memory_limit || -1 === (int) $memory_limit) {
            return PHP_INT_MAX;
        }

        return wp_convert_hr_to_bytes($memory_limit);
    }

    /**
     * Check if time limit exceeded
     */
    private function time_exceeded() {
        $time_limit = ini_get('max_execution_time');
        
        if (!$time_limit || $time_limit === 0) {
            return false;
        }

        $start_time = defined('WP_START_TIMESTAMP') ? WP_START_TIMESTAMP : time();
        return (time() - $start_time) >= ($time_limit * 0.8);
    }

    /**
     * Optimize database tables
     */
    public function optimize_tables() {
        global $wpdb;

        $tables = [
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tasks',
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_logs',
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_users',
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tenants'
        ];

        foreach ($tables as $table) {
            $wpdb->query("OPTIMIZE TABLE $table");
        }
    }

    /**
     * Clear old data
     */
    public function clear_old_data($days = 30) {
        global $wpdb;

        // Clear old tasks
        $wpdb->query($wpdb->prepare(
            "DELETE FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks
            WHERE status IN ('completed', 'failed', 'cancelled')
            AND created_at < DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL %d DAY)",
            $days
        ));

        // Clear old logs
        $wpdb->query($wpdb->prepare(
            "DELETE FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_logs
            WHERE created_at < DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL %d DAY)",
            $days
        ));
    }
}

檔名：class-logger.php

<?php
namespace AIMagic;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

class Logger {
    const ERROR = 'error';
    const WARNING = 'warning';
    const INFO = 'info';
    const DEBUG = 'debug';

    private $settings;
    private $log_retention;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->settings = get_option('aimagic_settings', []);
        $this->log_retention = $this->settings['monitoring']['log_retention'] ?? 30;

        add_action('aimagic_daily_maintenance', [$this, 'cleanup_old_logs']);
    }

    /**
     * Log a message
     */
    public function log($level, $message, $context = []) {
        if (!$this->settings['monitoring']['enable_logging']) {
            return false;
        }

        global $wpdb;

        $data = [
            'level' => $level,
            'message' => $message,
            'context' => is_array($context) ? json_encode($context) : $context,
            'created_at' => current_time('mysql')
        ];

        if (isset($context['tenant_id'])) {
            $data['tenant_id'] = $context['tenant_id'];
        }

        if (isset($context['user_id'])) {
            $data['user_id'] = $context['user_id'];
        }

        $result = $wpdb->insert(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_logs',
            $data,
            ['%s', '%s', '%s', '%s', '%d', '%d']
        );

        if ($result && $level === self::ERROR) {
            $this->notify_admin($message, $context);
        }

        return $result;
    }

    /**
     * Log an error
     */
    public function error($message, $context = []) {
        return $this->log(self::ERROR, $message, $context);
    }

    /**
     * Log a warning
     */
    public function warning($message, $context = []) {
        return $this->log(self::WARNING, $message, $context);
    }

    /**
     * Log an info message
     */
    public function info($message, $context = []) {
        return $this->log(self::INFO, $message, $context);
    }

    /**
     * Log a debug message
     */
    public function debug($message, $context = []) {
        return $this->log(self::DEBUG, $message, $context);
    }

    /**
     * Clean up old logs
     */
    public function cleanup_old_logs() {
        global $wpdb;

        return $wpdb->query($wpdb->prepare(
            "DELETE FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_logs
            WHERE created_at < DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL %d DAY)",
            $this->log_retention
        ));
    }

    /**
     * Notify admin of errors
     */
    private function notify_admin($message, $context) {
        $alert_threshold = $this->settings['monitoring']['alert_threshold'] ?? 10;
        $notify_email = $this->settings['monitoring']['notify_email'] ?? get_option('admin_email');

        // Count recent errors
        global $wpdb;
        $recent_errors = $wpdb->get_var($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT COUNT(*)
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_logs
            WHERE level = 'error'
            AND created_at > DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 1 HOUR)"
        ));

        if ($recent_errors >= $alert_threshold) {
            $subject = sprintf(
                __('[%s] Alert: High Error Rate Detected', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                get_bloginfo('name')
            );

            $body = sprintf(
                __("High error rate detected in AI Magic Publisher.\n\nLatest error: %s\n\nContext: %s\n\nTotal errors in last hour: %d", 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                $message,
                json_encode($context, JSON_PRETTY_PRINT),
                $recent_errors
            );

            wp_mail($notify_email, $subject, $body);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get logs with filtering
     */
    public function get_logs($args = []) {
        global $wpdb;

        $defaults = [
            'level' => '',
            'tenant_id' => 0,
            'user_id' => 0,
            'start_date' => '',
            'end_date' => '',
            'search' => '',
            'orderby' => 'created_at',
            'order' => 'DESC',
            'per_page' => 20,
            'page' => 1
        ];

        $args = wp_parse_args($args, $defaults);
        $where = [];
        $values = [];

        if ($args['level']) {
            $where[] = 'level = %s';
            $values[] = $args['level'];
        }

        if ($args['tenant_id']) {
            $where[] = 'tenant_id = %d';
            $values[] = $args['tenant_id'];
        }

        if ($args['user_id']) {
            $where[] = 'user_id = %d';
            $values[] = $args['user_id'];
        }

        if ($args['start_date']) {
            $where[] = 'created_at >= %s';
            $values[] = $args['start_date'];
        }

        if ($args['end_date']) {
            $where[] = 'created_at <= %s';
            $values[] = $args['end_date'];
        }

        if ($args['search']) {
            $where[] = '(message LIKE %s OR context LIKE %s)';
            $search_term = '%' . $wpdb->esc_like($args['search']) . '%';
            $values[] = $search_term;
            $values[] = $search_term;
        }

        $where_clause = !empty($where) ? 'WHERE ' . implode(' AND ', $where) : '';
        $offset = ($args['page'] - 1) * $args['per_page'];

        $query = $wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT SQL_CALC_FOUND_ROWS *
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_logs
            $where_clause
            ORDER BY {$args['orderby']} {$args['order']}
            LIMIT %d OFFSET %d",
            array_merge($values, [$args['per_page'], $offset])
        );

        $results = [
            'logs' => $wpdb->get_results($query),
            'total' => $wpdb->get_var('SELECT FOUND_ROWS()')
        ];

        return $results;
    }
}

目錄：/www/wwwroot/xart004.heatgroups.top/wp-content/plugins/ai_plateform_v2/files_2025/includes/api

<?php
namespace AIMagic\API;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

class API {
    private $namespace = 'aimagic/v1';
    private $gpt4;
    private $line;
    private $wechat;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->gpt4 = new \AIMagic\Integrations\GPT4Integration();
        $this->line = new \AIMagic\Integrations\LINEIntegration();
        $this->wechat = new \AIMagic\Integrations\WeChatIntegration();
    }

    /**
     * Register REST API routes
     */
    public function register_routes() {
        // Webhook endpoints
        register_rest_route($this->namespace, '/webhook/line', [
            [
                'methods' => 'POST',
                'callback' => [$this, 'handle_line_webhook'],
                'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_line_webhook']
            ]
        ]);

        register_rest_route($this->namespace, '/webhook/wechat', [
            [
                'methods' => ['GET', 'POST'],
                'callback' => [$this, 'handle_wechat_webhook'],
                'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_wechat_webhook']
            ]
        ]);

        // Content generation endpoints
        register_rest_route($this->namespace, '/generate', [
            [
                'methods' => 'POST',
                'callback' => [$this, 'generate_content'],
                'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_api_key'],
                'args' => [
                    'prompt' => [
                        'required' => true,
                        'type' => 'string',
                        'sanitize_callback' => 'sanitize_text_field'
                    ],
                    'max_tokens' => [
                        'type' => 'integer',
                        'default' => 2048,
                        'minimum' => 1,
                        'maximum' => 4096
                    ],
                    'temperature' => [
                        'type' => 'number',
                        'default' => 0.7,
                        'minimum' => 0,
                        'maximum' => 1
                    ]
                ]
            ]
        ]);

        // Task management endpoints
        register_rest_route($this->namespace, '/tasks', [
            [
                'methods' => 'GET',
                'callback' => [$this, 'get_tasks'],
                'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_api_key']
            ],
            [
                'methods' => 'POST',
                'callback' => [$this, 'create_task'],
                'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_api_key'],
                'args' => [
                    'type' => [
                        'required' => true,
                        'type' => 'string',
                        'enum' => ['content_generation', 'image_generation', 'translation', 'summarization', 'analysis']
                    ],
                    'content' => [
                        'required' => true,
                        'type' => 'string'
                    ]
                ]
            ]
        ]);

        register_rest_route($this->namespace, '/tasks/(?P<id>\d+)', [
            [
                'methods' => 'GET',
                'callback' => [$this, 'get_task'],
                'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_api_key']
            ],
            [
                'methods' => 'DELETE',
                'callback' => [$this, 'delete_task'],
                'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_api_key']
            ]
        ]);

        // User management endpoints
        register_rest_route($this->namespace, '/users/me', [
            [
                'methods' => 'GET',
                'callback' => [$this, 'get_current_user'],
                'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_api_key']
            ]
        ]);

        // Stats endpoints
        register_rest_route($this->namespace, '/stats', [
            [
                'methods' => 'GET',
                'callback' => [$this, 'get_stats'],
                'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_api_key']
            ]
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Verify LINE webhook signature
     */
    public function verify_line_webhook(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        $signature = $request->get_header('X-Line-Signature');
        return $this->line->verify_signature($signature, $request->get_body());
    }

    /**
     * Handle LINE webhook
     */
    public function handle_line_webhook(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        $body = json_decode($request->get_body(), true);
        $results = $this->line->handle_webhook($body);

        return new \WP_REST_Response([
            'success' => true,
            'results' => $results
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Verify WeChat webhook
     */
    public function verify_wechat_webhook(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        if ($request->get_method() === 'GET') {
            $params = $request->get_params();
            return $this->wechat->verify_signature(
                $params['signature'],
                $params['timestamp'],
                $params['nonce']
            );
        }
        return true;
    }

    /**
     * Handle WeChat webhook
     */
    public function handle_wechat_webhook(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        if ($request->get_method() === 'GET') {
            return new \WP_REST_Response($request->get_param('echostr'));
        }

        $xml = $request->get_body();
        $response = $this->wechat->handle_webhook($xml);

        return new \WP_REST_Response($response);
    }

    /**
     * Verify API key
     */
    public function verify_api_key(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        $api_key = $request->get_header('X-API-Key');
        if (empty($api_key)) {
            return new \WP_Error(
                'missing_api_key',
                __('API key is required', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                ['status' => 401]
            );
        }

        global $wpdb;
        $tenant = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants WHERE api_key = %s AND status = 'active'",
            $api_key
        ));

        if (!$tenant) {
            return new \WP_Error(
                'invalid_api_key',
                __('Invalid or inactive API key', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                ['status' => 401]
            );
        }

        // Store tenant ID for later use
        $request->set_param('tenant_id', $tenant->id);
        return true;
    }

    /**
     * Generate content
     */
    public function generate_content(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        $params = $request->get_params();
        $response = $this->gpt4->generate_content($params['prompt'], [
            'max_tokens' => $params['max_tokens'],
            'temperature' => $params['temperature']
        ]);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            return $response;
        }

        // Create task record
        $task_id = $this->create_task([
            'tenant_id' => $request->get_param('tenant_id'),
            'type' => 'content_generation',
            'content' => $params['prompt'],
            'result' => $response['content']
        ]);

        if (is_wp_error($task_id)) {
            return $task_id;
        }

        return new \WP_REST_Response([
            'success' => true,
            'task_id' => $task_id,
            'content' => $response['content'],
            'usage' => $response['usage']
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Get tasks
     */
    public function get_tasks(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        global $wpdb;

        $tenant_id = $request->get_param('tenant_id');
        $page = $request->get_param('page') ?: 1;
        $per_page = $request->get_param('per_page') ?: 20;
        $status = $request->get_param('status');

        $where = ['tenant_id = %d'];
        $values = [$tenant_id];

        if ($status) {
            $where[] = 'status = %s';
            $values[] = $status;
        }

        $where_clause = 'WHERE ' . implode(' AND ', $where);
        $offset = ($page - 1) * $per_page;

        $tasks = $wpdb->get_results($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks
            $where_clause
            ORDER BY created_at DESC
            LIMIT %d OFFSET %d",
            array_merge($values, [$per_page, $offset])
        ));

        $total = $wpdb->get_var($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks $where_clause",
            $values
        ));

        return new \WP_REST_Response([
            'success' => true,
            'tasks' => $tasks,
            'total' => (int) $total,
            'pages' => ceil($total / $per_page)
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Get single task
     */
    public function get_task(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        global $wpdb;

        $task = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks
            WHERE id = %d AND tenant_id = %d",
            $request->get_param('id'),
            $request->get_param('tenant_id')
        ));

        if (!$task) {
            return new \WP_Error(
                'task_not_found',
                __('Task not found', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                ['status' => 404]
            );
        }

        return new \WP_REST_Response([
            'success' => true,
            'task' => $task
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Delete task
     */
    public function delete_task(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        global $wpdb;

        $result = $wpdb->delete(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tasks',
            [
                'id' => $request->get_param('id'),
                'tenant_id' => $request->get_param('tenant_id')
            ],
            ['%d', '%d']
        );

        if ($result === false) {
            return new \WP_Error(
                'delete_failed',
                __('Failed to delete task', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                ['status' => 500]
            );
        }

        return new \WP_REST_Response([
            'success' => true,
            'message' => __('Task deleted successfully', 'ai-magic-publisher')
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Get current user stats
     */
    public function get_current_user(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        global $wpdb;

        $tenant_id = $request->get_param('tenant_id');
        
        $stats = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT 
                COUNT(DISTINCT t.id) as total_tasks,
                SUM(CASE WHEN t.status = 'completed' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as completed_tasks,
                SUM(CASE WHEN t.status = 'failed' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as failed_tasks,
                MAX(t.created_at) as last_task_date
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks t
            WHERE t.tenant_id = %d",
            $tenant_id
        ));

        $quota = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT quota_used, quota_limit
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants
            WHERE id = %d",
            $tenant_id
        ));

        return new \WP_REST_Response([
            'success' => true,
            'stats' => $stats,
            'quota' => $quota
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Get usage statistics
     */
    public function get_stats(\WP_REST_Request $request) {
        global $wpdb;

        $tenant_id = $request->get_param('tenant_id');
        $period = $request->get_param('period') ?: '7days';

        switch ($period) {
            case '24hours':
                $interval = '1 HOUR';
                $group_format = '%Y-%m-%d %H:00:00';
                $where = 'created_at >= DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 24 HOUR)';
                break;
            case '7days':
                $interval = '1 DAY';
                $group_format = '%Y-%m-%d';
                $where = 'created_at >= DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 7 DAY)';
                break;
            case '30days':
                $interval = '1 DAY';
                $group_format = '%Y-%m-%d';
                $where = 'created_at >= DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 30 DAY)';
                break;
            default:
                return new \WP_Error(
                    'invalid_period',
                    __('Invalid period specified', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    ['status' => 400]
                );
        }

        $stats = $wpdb->get_results($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT 
                DATE_FORMAT(created_at, %s) as date,
                COUNT(*) as total,
                SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'completed' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as completed,
                SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'failed' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as failed
            FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks
            WHERE tenant_id = %d AND $where
            GROUP BY date
            ORDER BY date ASC",
            $group_format,
            $tenant_id
        ));

        return new \WP_REST_Response([
            'success' => true,
            'stats' => $stats
        ]);
    }
}

檔名：class-background-process.php
==================================================
<?php
namespace AIMagic;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

abstract class BackgroundProcess {
    protected $action = 'background_process';
    protected $prefix = 'wp_';
    protected $identifier;

    /**
     * Initialize background process
     */
    public function __construct() {
        $this->identifier = $this->prefix . $this->action;

        add_action('wp_ajax_' . $this->identifier, [$this, 'handle_cron']);
        add_action('wp_ajax_nopriv_' . $this->identifier, [$this, 'handle_cron']);
        add_action($this->identifier . '_cron', [$this, 'handle_cron']);
    }

    /**
     * Schedule event
     */
    protected function schedule_event() {
        if (!wp_next_scheduled($this->identifier . '_cron')) {
            wp_schedule_event(time(), 'every_minute', $this->identifier . '_cron');
        }
    }

    /**
     * Clear scheduled event
     */
    protected function clear_scheduled_event() {
        wp_clear_scheduled_hook($this->identifier . '_cron');
    }

    /**
     * Handle cron event
     */
    public function handle_cron() {
        $this->process_queue();
        die();
    }

    /**
     * Process queue
     */
    protected function process_queue() {
        if ($this->is_process_running()) {
            return;
        }

        $this->lock_process();

        try {
            $this->task_runner();
        } finally {
            $this->unlock_process();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Task runner
     */
    protected function task_runner() {
        $tasks = $this->get_batch();

        foreach ($tasks as $task) {
            $result = $this->process_task($task);

            if ($result === false) {
                break;
            }

            $this->delete_task($task);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get batch of tasks
     */
    abstract protected function get_batch();

    /**
     * Process single task
     */
    abstract protected function process_task($task);

    /**
     * Delete task
     */
    abstract protected function delete_task($task);

    /**
     * Check if process is running
     */
    protected function is_process_running() {
        return (bool) get_site_transient($this->identifier . '_process_lock');
    }

    /**
     * Lock process
     */
    protected function lock_process() {
        set_site_transient($this->identifier . '_process_lock', microtime(), 60);
    }

    /**
     * Unlock process
     */
    protected function unlock_process() {
        delete_site_transient($this->identifier . '_process_lock');
    }

    /**
     * Memory exceeded
     */
    protected function memory_exceeded() {
        $memory_limit = $this->get_memory_limit() * 0.9;
        $current_memory = memory_get_usage(true);
        return $current_memory >= $memory_limit;
    }

    /**
     * Get memory limit
     */
    protected function get_memory_limit() {
        if (function_exists('ini_get')) {
            $memory_limit = ini_get('memory_limit');
        } else {
            $memory_limit = '128M';
        }

        if (!$memory_limit || -1 === (int) $memory_limit) {
            return PHP_INT_MAX;
        }

        return wp_convert_hr_to_bytes($memory_limit);
    }

    /**
     * Time exceeded
     */
    protected function time_exceeded() {
        $finish = $this->start_time + 20; // 20 seconds
        return time() >= $finish;
    }
}

<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class Roles {
    private static $instance = null;
    
    private $roles = [
        'aimagic_admin' => [
            'name' => 'AI Magic Admin',
            'capabilities' => [
                'manage_aimagic_settings',
                'manage_aimagic_tenants',
                'manage_aimagic_users',
                'manage_aimagic_tasks',
                'view_aimagic_reports',
                'manage_aimagic_webhooks',
                'adjust_aimagic_quotas'
            ]
        ],
        'aimagic_manager' => [
            'name' => 'AI Magic Manager',
            'capabilities' => [
                'manage_aimagic_tasks',
                'view_aimagic_reports',
                'manage_aimagic_users'
            ]
        ],
        'aimagic_user' => [
            'name' => 'AI Magic User',
            'capabilities' => [
                'create_aimagic_tasks',
                'view_own_aimagic_tasks'
            ]
        ]
    ];

    private $capabilities = [
        'manage_aimagic_settings' => 'Manage AI Magic Settings',
        'manage_aimagic_tenants' => 'Manage Tenants',
        'manage_aimagic_users' => 'Manage Users',
        'manage_aimagic_tasks' => 'Manage All Tasks',
        'create_aimagic_tasks' => 'Create Tasks',
        'view_own_aimagic_tasks' => 'View Own Tasks',
        'view_aimagic_reports' => 'View Reports',
        'manage_aimagic_webhooks' => 'Manage Webhooks',
        'adjust_aimagic_quotas' => 'Adjust Quotas'
    ];

    public static function get_instance() {
        if (null === self::$instance) {
            self::$instance = new self();
        }
        return self::$instance;
    }

    public function init() {
        add_action('admin_init', [$this, 'add_roles_and_capabilities']);
        add_filter('user_has_cap', [$this, 'filter_user_capabilities'], 10, 4);
    }

    public function add_roles_and_capabilities() {
        global $wp_roles;

        if (!isset($wp_roles)) {
            $wp_roles = new \WP_Roles();
        }

        // Add capabilities to administrator role
        $admin_role = get_role('administrator');
        if ($admin_role) {
            foreach ($this->capabilities as $cap => $label) {
                $admin_role->add_cap($cap);
            }
        }

        // Add custom roles
        foreach ($this->roles as $role_id => $role_data) {
            if (!$wp_roles->is_role($role_id)) {
                add_role($role_id, $role_data['name'], array_fill_keys($role_data['capabilities'], true));
            }
        }
    }

    public function filter_user_capabilities($allcaps, $caps, $args, $user) {
        // If not logged in, return default caps
        if (!$user->ID) {
            return $allcaps;
        }

        // Get user's tenant ID
        $tenant_id = get_user_meta($user->ID, 'aimagic_tenant_id', true);

        // Handle tenant-specific capabilities
        foreach ($caps as $cap) {
            switch ($cap) {
                case 'view_own_aimagic_tasks':
                    $allcaps[$cap] = true;
                    break;

                case 'create_aimagic_tasks':
                    // Check if user's tenant has available quota
                    if ($tenant_id && $this->tenant_has_quota($tenant_id)) {
                        $allcaps[$cap] = true;
                    }
                    break;

                case 'manage_aimagic_tasks':
                    // Managers can only manage tasks within their tenant
                    if (isset($allcaps[$cap]) && $allcaps[$cap] && !current_user_can('manage_aimagic_settings')) {
                        $task_id = isset($args[2]) ? $args[2] : 0;
                        if ($task_id && !$this->can_manage_task($user->ID, $task_id)) {
                            $allcaps[$cap] = false;
                        }
                    }
                    break;
            }
        }

        return $allcaps;
    }

    private function tenant_has_quota($tenant_id) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        $tenant = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT quota_used, quota_limit FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants WHERE id = %d AND status = 'active'",
            $tenant_id
        ));

        return $tenant && $tenant->quota_used < $tenant->quota_limit;
    }

    private function can_manage_task($user_id, $task_id) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        $tenant_id = get_user_meta($user_id, 'aimagic_tenant_id', true);
        if (!$tenant_id) return false;

        $task_tenant = $wpdb->get_var($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT tenant_id FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks WHERE id = %d",
            $task_id
        ));

        return $task_tenant == $tenant_id;
    }

    public function get_roles() {
        return $this->roles;
    }

    public function get_capabilities() {
        return $this->capabilities;
    }

    public static function remove_roles_and_capabilities() {
        global $wp_roles;

        if (!isset($wp_roles)) {
            $wp_roles = new \WP_Roles();
        }

        $instance = self::get_instance();

        // Remove capabilities from administrator
        $admin_role = get_role('administrator');
        if ($admin_role) {
            foreach ($instance->capabilities as $cap => $label) {
                $admin_role->remove_cap($cap);
            }
        }

        // Remove custom roles
        foreach ($instance->roles as $role_id => $role_data) {
            remove_role($role_id);
        }
    }
}

檔名：class-webhook-handler (2).php

<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class WebhookHandler {
    private $secret;
    private $logger;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->secret = get_option('aimagic_webhook_secret');
        $this->logger = new Logger();
    }

    public function init() {
        add_action('rest_api_init', [$this, 'register_webhook_endpoint']);
    }

    public function register_webhook_endpoint() {
        register_rest_route('aimagic/v1', '/webhook', [
            'methods' => 'POST',
            'callback' => [$this, 'handle_webhook'],
            'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_webhook_signature']
        ]);
    }

    public function verify_webhook_signature($request) {
        $signature = $request->get_header('X-Aimagic-Signature');
        if (!$signature) {
            $this->logger->error('Missing webhook signature');
            return false;
        }

        $payload = $request->get_body();
        $expected_signature = hash_hmac('sha256', $payload, $this->secret);

        if (!hash_equals($expected_signature, $signature)) {
            $this->logger->error('Invalid webhook signature');
            return false;
        }

        return true;
    }

    public function handle_webhook($request) {
        try {
            $payload = $request->get_json_params();
            
            if (!isset($payload['event']) || !isset($payload['data'])) {
                throw new \Exception('Invalid webhook payload format');
            }

            switch ($payload['event']) {
                case 'task.completed':
                    return $this->handle_task_completed($payload['data']);
                
                case 'task.failed':
                    return $this->handle_task_failed($payload['data']);
                
                case 'quota.exceeded':
                    return $this->handle_quota_exceeded($payload['data']);
                
                default:
                    throw new \Exception('Unknown webhook event: ' . $payload['event']);
            }
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $this->logger->error('Webhook error: ' . $e->getMessage());
            return new \WP_Error(
                'webhook_error',
                $e->getMessage(),
                ['status' => 400]
            );
        }
    }

    private function handle_task_completed($data) {
        global $wpdb;

        // Start transaction
        $wpdb->query('START TRANSACTION');

        try {
            // Update task status
            $updated = $wpdb->update(
                $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tasks',
                [
                    'status' => 'completed',
                    'result' => sanitize_textarea_field($data['result']),
                    'completed_at' => current_time('mysql'),
                    'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
                ],
                ['id' => intval($data['task_id'])],
                ['%s', '%s', '%s', '%s'],
                ['%d']
            );

            if ($updated === false) {
                throw new \Exception('Failed to update task status');
            }

            // Update quota usage
            $bytes_used = intval($data['bytes_used']);
            if ($bytes_used > 0) {
                $updated = $wpdb->query($wpdb->prepare(
                    "UPDATE {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants
                    SET quota_used = quota_used + %d,
                        updated_at = %s
                    WHERE id = (
                        SELECT tenant_id 
                        FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks 
                        WHERE id = %d
                    )",
                    $bytes_used,
                    current_time('mysql'),
                    intval($data['task_id'])
                ));

                if ($updated === false) {
                    throw new \Exception('Failed to update quota usage');
                }
            }

            // Send email notification
            $task = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
                "SELECT t.*, u.user_email 
                FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks t
                LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->users} u ON t.user_id = u.ID
                WHERE t.id = %d",
                intval($data['task_id'])
            ));

            if ($task && $task->user_email) {
                wp_mail(
                    $task->user_email,
                    __('Task Completed', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    sprintf(
                        __('Your task #%d has been completed. Click here to view the results: %s', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                        $task->id,
                        admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tasks&action=view&id=' . $task->id)
                    )
                );
            }

            $wpdb->query('COMMIT');
            
            $this->logger->info('Task completed successfully', ['task_id' => $data['task_id']]);
            
            return new \WP_REST_Response(['status' => 'success'], 200);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $wpdb->query('ROLLBACK');
            
            $this->logger->error('Task completion failed: ' . $e->getMessage(), [
                'task_id' => $data['task_id']
            ]);
            
            return new \WP_Error(
                'task_completion_failed',
                $e->getMessage(),
                ['status' => 500]
            );
        }
    }

    private function handle_task_failed($data) {
        global $wpdb;

        $updated = $wpdb->update(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tasks',
            [
                'status' => 'failed',
                'error_message' => sanitize_textarea_field($data['error']),
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['id' => intval($data['task_id'])],
            ['%s', '%s', '%s'],
            ['%d']
        );

        if ($updated === false) {
            $this->logger->error('Failed to update task status', [
                'task_id' => $data['task_id']
            ]);
            return new \WP_Error(
                'update_failed',
                'Failed to update task status',
                ['status' => 500]
            );
        }

        $this->logger->error('Task failed', [
            'task_id' => $data['task_id'],
            'error' => $data['error']
        ]);

        return new \WP_REST_Response(['status' => 'success'], 200);
    }

    private function handle_quota_exceeded($data) {
        global $wpdb;

        // Update tenant status
        $wpdb->update(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tenants',
            [
                'status' => 'quota_exceeded',
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['id' => intval($data['tenant_id'])],
            ['%s', '%s'],
            ['%d']
        );

        // Send notification to admin
        $tenant = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants WHERE id = %d",
            intval($data['tenant_id'])
        ));

        if ($tenant) {
            wp_mail(
                get_option('admin_email'),
                __('Quota Exceeded Alert', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                sprintf(
                    __('Tenant "%s" has exceeded their quota limit. Please review their usage and adjust the quota if needed.', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    $tenant->name
                )
            );
        }

        $this->logger->warning('Quota exceeded', [
            'tenant_id' => $data['tenant_id'],
            'quota_used' => $data['quota_used'],
            'quota_limit' => $data['quota_limit']
        ]);

        return new \WP_REST_Response(['status' => 'success'], 200);
    }
}

檔名：class-task-queue.php

<?php
namespace AIMagic;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

class TaskQueue {
    private $batch_size = 10;
    private $lock_timeout = 300; // 5 minutes

    /**
     * Initialize the task queue
     */
    public function __construct() {
        add_action('aimagic_process_queue', [$this, 'process_queue']);
        
        if (!wp_next_scheduled('aimagic_process_queue')) {
            wp_schedule_event(time(), 'every_minute', 'aimagic_process_queue');
        }
    }

    /**
     * Add a task to the queue
     */
    public function add_task($data) {
        global $wpdb;

        $defaults = [
            'tenant_id' => 0,
            'user_id' => get_current_user_id(),
            'type' => '',
            'content' => '',
            'status' => 'pending',
            'priority' => 1,
            'created_at' => current_time('mysql'),
            'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
        ];

        $data = wp_parse_args($data, $defaults);

        $result = $wpdb->insert(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tasks',
            $data,
            [
                '%d', '%d', '%s', '%s', '%s', 
                '%d', '%s', '%s'
            ]
        );

        if (!$result) {
            return new \WP_Error(
                'task_creation_failed',
                __('Failed to create task', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            );
        }

        do_action('aimagic_task_added', $wpdb->insert_id, $data);

        return $wpdb->insert_id;
    }

    /**
     * Process the task queue
     */
    public function process_queue() {
        if (!$this->acquire_lock()) {
            return;
        }

        try {
            $tasks = $this->get_pending_tasks();
            
            foreach ($tasks as $task) {
                $this->process_task($task);
            }
        } finally {
            $this->release_lock();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get pending tasks
     */
    private function get_pending_tasks() {
        global $wpdb;

        return $wpdb->get_results($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks
            WHERE status = 'pending'
            ORDER BY priority DESC, created_at ASC
            LIMIT %d",
            $this->batch_size
        ));
    }

    /**
     * Process a single task
     */
    private function process_task($task) {
        global $wpdb;

        // Update task status to running
        $wpdb->update(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tasks',
            [
                'status' => 'running',
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['id' => $task->id],
            ['%s', '%s'],
            ['%d']
        );

        try {
            $result = $this->execute_task($task);

            $update = [
                'status' => 'completed',
                'result' => $result,
                'completed_at' => current_time('mysql'),
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ];
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $update = [
                'status' => 'failed',
                'error_message' => $e->getMessage(),
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ];
        }

        // Update task status
        $wpdb->update(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tasks',
            $update,
            ['id' => $task->id]
        );

        do_action('aimagic_task_completed', $task->id, $update);
    }

    /**
     * Execute a task based on its type
     */
    private function execute_task($task) {
        switch ($task->type) {
            case 'content_generation':
                return $this->generate_content($task);
            
            case 'image_generation':
                return $this->generate_image($task);
            
            case 'translation':
                return $this->translate_content($task);
            
            case 'summarization':
                return $this->summarize_content($task);
            
            case 'analysis':
                return $this->analyze_content($task);
            
            default:
                throw new \Exception(__('Unknown task type', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }
    }

    /**
     * Generate content using GPT-4
     */
    private function generate_content($task) {
        $gpt4 = new \AIMagic\Integrations\GPT4Integration();
        $response = $gpt4->generate_content($task->content);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            throw new \Exception($response->get_error_message());
        }

        return $response['content'];
    }

    /**
     * Generate image
     */
    private function generate_image($task) {
        // Implementation for image generation
        throw new \Exception(__('Image generation not implemented yet', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
    }

    /**
     * Translate content
     */
    private function translate_content($task) {
        $content = json_decode($task->content, true);
        if (!isset($content['text'], $content['target_language'])) {
            throw new \Exception(__('Invalid translation request', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }

        $prompt = sprintf(
            'Translate the following text to %s:\n\n%s',
            $content['target_language'],
            $content['text']
        );

        $gpt4 = new \AIMagic\Integrations\GPT4Integration();
        $response = $gpt4->generate_content($prompt);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            throw new \Exception($response->get_error_message());
        }

        return $response['content'];
    }

    /**
     * Summarize content
     */
    private function summarize_content($task) {
        $content = json_decode($task->content, true);
        $length = $content['length'] ?? 'medium';

        $prompt = sprintf(
            'Summarize the following text. Length: %s\n\n%s',
            $length,
            is_array($content) ? $content['text'] : $task->content
        );

        $gpt4 = new \AIMagic\Integrations\GPT4Integration();
        $response = $gpt4->generate_content($prompt);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            throw new \Exception($response->get_error_message());
        }

        return $response['content'];
    }

    /**
     * Analyze content
     */
    private function analyze_content($task) {
        $content = json_decode($task->content, true);
        $type = $content['analysis_type'] ?? 'general';

        $prompts = [
            'general' => 'Analyze the following content and provide insights:\n\n',
            'sentiment' => 'Perform sentiment analysis on the following text:\n\n',
            'seo' => 'Analyze the following content for SEO optimization:\n\n',
            'readability' => 'Analyze the readability of the following content:\n\n'
        ];

        $prompt = ($prompts[$type] ?? $prompts['general']) . 
                 (is_array($content) ? $content['text'] : $task->content);

        $gpt4 = new \AIMagic\Integrations\GPT4Integration();
        $response = $gpt4->generate_content($prompt);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            throw new \Exception($response->get_error_message());
        }

        return $response['content'];
    }

    /**
     * Acquire lock for queue processing
     */
    private function acquire_lock() {
        global $wpdb;

        $lock_name = 'aimagic_queue_lock';
        $now = time();
        $lock_timeout = $now + $this->lock_timeout;

        $current_lock = get_transient($lock_name);
        if ($current_lock && $current_lock > $now) {
            return false;
        }

        set_transient($lock_name, $lock_timeout, $this->lock_timeout);
        return true;
    }

    /**
     * Release queue processing lock
     */
    private function release_lock() {
        delete_transient('aimagic_queue_lock');
    }
}

檔名：class-auth-middleware.php

<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class AuthMiddleware {
    private $session_manager;
    private $rate_limiter;
    private $logger;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->session_manager = new SessionManager();
        $this->rate_limiter = new RateLimiter();
        $this->logger = new Logger();
    }

    public function init() {
        add_filter('authenticate', [$this, 'check_login_attempts'], 30, 3);
        add_action('wp_login_failed', [$this, 'track_failed_login']);
        add_action('wp_login', [$this, 'track_successful_login'], 10, 2);
        add_action('init', [$this, 'initialize_session']);
        add_action('admin_init', [$this, 'verify_session']);
    }

    public function check_login_attempts($user, $username, $password) {
        if (empty($username) || empty($password)) {
            return $user;
        }

        $ip = $this->get_client_ip();
        
        // Check if IP is blocked
        if (!$this->rate_limiter->check('login_' . $ip, 5, 900)) { // 5 attempts per 15 minutes
            $this->logger->warning('Login attempt blocked due to rate limit', [
                'ip' => $ip,
                'username' => $username
            ]);
            
            return new \WP_Error(
                'too_many_attempts',
                __('Too many failed login attempts. Please try again later.', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            );
        }

        return $user;
    }

    public function track_failed_login($username) {
        $ip = $this->get_client_ip();
        
        $this->logger->warning('Failed login attempt', [
            'ip' => $ip,
            'username' => $username
        ]);

        // Store failed attempt in database
        global $wpdb;
        $wpdb->insert(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_login_attempts',
            [
                'username' => $username,
                'ip_address' => $ip,
                'status' => 'failed',
                'created_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['%s', '%s', '%s', '%s']
        );
    }

    public function track_successful_login($username, $user) {
        $ip = $this->get_client_ip();
        
        $this->logger->info('Successful login', [
            'ip' => $ip,
            'user_id' => $user->ID
        ]);

        // Reset failed attempts counter
        $this->rate_limiter->reset('login_' . $ip);

        // Store successful login in database
        global $wpdb;
        $wpdb->insert(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_login_attempts',
            [
                'username' => $username,
                'ip_address' => $ip,
                'status' => 'success',
                'created_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['%s', '%s', '%s', '%s']
        );

        // Initialize secure session
        $this->session_manager->create_session($user->ID);
    }

    public function initialize_session() {
        if (!$this->session_manager->is_valid_session()) {
            $this->session_manager->start_session();
        }
    }

    public function verify_session() {
        if (!$this->session_manager->verify_session()) {
            wp_logout();
            wp_redirect(wp_login_url());
            exit;
        }
    }

    private function get_client_ip() {
        $ip = '';
        
        if (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_CF_CONNECTING_IP'])) { // Cloudflare
            $ip = $_SERVER['HTTP_CF_CONNECTING_IP'];
        } elseif (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_X_REAL_IP'])) { // Nginx proxy
            $ip = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_REAL_IP'];
        } elseif (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR'])) {
            // Get the first IP in case of multiple proxies
            $ip = trim(current(explode(',', $_SERVER['HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR'])));
        } elseif (isset($_SERVER['REMOTE_ADDR'])) {
            $ip = $_SERVER['REMOTE_ADDR'];
        }

        return filter_var($ip, FILTER_VALIDATE_IP) ? $ip : '';
    }
}

檔名：class-session-manager.php
==================================================
<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class SessionManager {
    private $session_name = 'aimagic_session';
    private $cookie_name = 'aimagic_session_token';
    private $session_duration = 3600; // 1 hour

    public function start_session() {
        if (session_status() === PHP_SESSION_NONE) {
            // Configure secure session settings
            ini_set('session.cookie_httponly', 1);
            ini_set('session.cookie_secure', is_ssl());
            ini_set('session.use_only_cookies', 1);
            ini_set('session.cookie_samesite', 'Strict');

            session_name($this->session_name);
            session_start();
        }
    }

    public function create_session($user_id) {
        $token = $this->generate_session_token();
        $expiration = time() + $this->session_duration;

        $_SESSION['user_id'] = $user_id;
        $_SESSION['token'] = $token;
        $_SESSION['expiration'] = $expiration;
        $_SESSION['ip'] = $this->get_client_ip();
        $_SESSION['user_agent'] = $_SERVER['HTTP_USER_AGENT'];

        // Store session in database
        $this->store_session([
            'user_id' => $user_id,
            'token' => $token,
            'ip_address' => $_SESSION['ip'],
            'user_agent' => $_SESSION['user_agent'],
            'expires_at' => date('Y-m-d H:i:s', $expiration)
        ]);

        // Set secure cookie
        $this->set_session_cookie($token, $expiration);
    }

    public function verify_session() {
        if (!isset($_SESSION['token']) || !isset($_COOKIE[$this->cookie_name])) {
            return false;
        }

        // Verify token matches
        if (!hash_equals($_SESSION['token'], $_COOKIE[$this->cookie_name])) {
            return false;
        }

        // Check expiration
        if ($_SESSION['expiration'] < time()) {
            $this->destroy_session();
            return false;
        }

        // Verify IP and user agent haven't changed
        if ($_SESSION['ip'] !== $this->get_client_ip() ||
            $_SESSION['user_agent'] !== $_SERVER['HTTP_USER_AGENT']) {
            $this->destroy_session();
            return false;
        }

        // Verify session exists in database
        if (!$this->verify_session_database($_SESSION['token'])) {
            $this->destroy_session();
            return false;
        }

        // Extend session if needed
        $this->extend_session();

        return true;
    }

    public function destroy_session() {
        if (isset($_SESSION['token'])) {
            $this->remove_session_database($_SESSION['token']);
        }

        session_unset();
        session_destroy();
        
        $this->remove_session_cookie();
    }

    public function is_valid_session() {
        return isset($_SESSION['token']) && $this->verify_session();
    }

    private function generate_session_token() {
        return bin2hex(random_bytes(32));
    }

    private function store_session($data) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        $wpdb->insert(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_sessions',
            $data,
            [
                '%d', // user_id
                '%s', // token
                '%s', // ip_address
                '%s', // user_agent
                '%s'  // expires_at
            ]
        );
    }

    private function verify_session_database($token) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        $session = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_sessions 
            WHERE token = %s AND expires_at > NOW()",
            $token
        ));

        return $session !== null;
    }

    private function remove_session_database($token) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        $wpdb->delete(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_sessions',
            ['token' => $token],
            ['%s']
        );
    }

    private function extend_session() {
        if ($_SESSION['expiration'] - time() < ($this->session_duration / 2)) {
            $expiration = time() + $this->session_duration;
            $_SESSION['expiration'] = $expiration;

            // Update database
            global $wpdb;
            $wpdb->update(
                $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_sessions',
                ['expires_at' => date('Y-m-d H:i:s', $expiration)],
                ['token' => $_SESSION['token']],
                ['%s'],
                ['%s']
            );

            // Update cookie
            $this->set_session_cookie($_SESSION['token'], $expiration);
        }
    }

    private function set_session_cookie($token, $expiration) {
        setcookie(
            $this->cookie_name,
            $token,
            $expiration,
            ADMIN_COOKIE_PATH,
            COOKIE_DOMAIN,
            is_ssl(),
            true
        );
    }

    private function remove_session_cookie() {
        setcookie(
            $this->cookie_name,
            '',
            time() - 3600,
            ADMIN_COOKIE_PATH,
            COOKIE_DOMAIN,
            is_ssl(),
            true
        );
    }

    private function get_client_ip() {
        $ip = '';
        
        if (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_CF_CONNECTING_IP'])) {
            $ip = $_SERVER['HTTP_CF_CONNECTING_IP'];
        } elseif (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_X_REAL_IP'])) {
            $ip = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_REAL_IP'];
        } elseif (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR'])) {
            $ip = trim(current(explode(',', $_SERVER['HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR'])));
        } elseif (isset($_SERVER['REMOTE_ADDR'])) {
            $ip = $_SERVER['REMOTE_ADDR'];
        }

        return filter_var($ip, FILTER_VALIDATE_IP) ? $ip : '';
    }
}

<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class Security {
    public static function sanitize_input($data, $type = 'text') {
        switch ($type) {
            case 'text':
                return sanitize_text_field($data);
            
            case 'textarea':
                return sanitize_textarea_field($data);
            
            case 'html':
                return wp_kses_post($data);
            
            case 'email':
                return sanitize_email($data);
            
            case 'url':
                return esc_url_raw($data);
            
            case 'int':
                return intval($data);
            
            case 'float':
                return floatval($data);
            
            case 'array':
                if (!is_array($data)) {
                    return [];
                }
                return array_map(function($item) {
                    return self::sanitize_input($item);
                }, $data);
            
            case 'json':
                if (is_string($data)) {
                    $decoded = json_decode($data, true);
                    if (json_last_error() === JSON_ERROR_NONE) {
                        return self::sanitize_input($decoded, 'array');
                    }
                }
                return null;
            
            default:
                return sanitize_text_field($data);
        }
    }

    public static function verify_api_key($api_key) {
        if (empty($api_key)) {
            return false;
        }

        global $wpdb;
        $tenant = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT id, status FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants WHERE api_key = %s",
            $api_key
        ));

        return $tenant && $tenant->status === 'active';
    }

    public static function generate_nonce($action = -1) {
        return wp_create_nonce("aimagic_" . $action);
    }

    public static function verify_nonce($nonce, $action = -1) {
        return wp_verify_nonce($nonce, "aimagic_" . $action);
    }

    public static function check_user_capabilities($capability) {
        if (!current_user_can($capability)) {
            wp_die(
                __('You do not have sufficient permissions to access this page.', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                403
            );
        }
    }

    public static function sanitize_sql_order($order) {
        $order = strtoupper($order);
        return in_array($order, ['ASC', 'DESC']) ? $order : 'DESC';
    }

    public static function sanitize_sql_orderby($orderby, $allowed_columns) {
        return in_array($orderby, $allowed_columns) ? $orderby : 'id';
    }

    public static function prepare_sql_where($where_conditions) {
        global $wpdb;
        
        $where = [];
        $values = [];
        
        foreach ($where_conditions as $condition) {
            if (isset($condition['column']) && isset($condition['value'])) {
                $operator = $condition['operator'] ?? '=';
                $where[] = $wpdb->prepare(
                    "`{$condition['column']}` $operator %s",
                    $condition['value']
                );
            }
        }
        
        return $where ? 'WHERE ' . implode(' AND ', $where) : '';
    }
}

<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class ErrorHandler {
    private $logger;
    private $last_error;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->logger = new Logger();
        $this->last_error = null;
    }

    public function init() {
        set_error_handler([$this, 'handle_error']);
        set_exception_handler([$this, 'handle_exception']);
        register_shutdown_function([$this, 'handle_shutdown']);
    }

    public function handle_error($errno, $errstr, $errfile, $errline) {
        if (!(error_reporting() & $errno)) {
            return false;
        }

        $error_data = [
            'type' => $errno,
            'message' => $errstr,
            'file' => $errfile,
            'line' => $errline
        ];

        switch ($errno) {
            case E_USER_ERROR:
                $this->logger->error('Fatal Error: ' . $errstr, $error_data);
                $this->display_error_page('Fatal Error');
                exit(1);

            case E_USER_WARNING:
                $this->logger->warning('Warning: ' . $errstr, $error_data);
                break;

            case E_USER_NOTICE:
                $this->logger->notice('Notice: ' . $errstr, $error_data);
                break;

            default:
                $this->logger->error('Unknown Error: ' . $errstr, $error_data);
                break;
        }

        $this->last_error = $error_data;
        return true;
    }

    public function handle_exception($exception) {
        $error_data = [
            'type' => get_class($exception),
            'message' => $exception->getMessage(),
            'file' => $exception->getFile(),
            'line' => $exception->getLine(),
            'trace' => $exception->getTraceAsString()
        ];

        $this->logger->error('Uncaught Exception: ' . $exception->getMessage(), $error_data);
        $this->last_error = $error_data;

        if (defined('DOING_AJAX')) {
            wp_send_json_error([
                'message' => __('An unexpected error occurred.', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                'error' => $exception->getMessage()
            ]);
        } else {
            $this->display_error_page('System Error');
        }
    }

    public function handle_shutdown() {
        $error = error_get_last();
        if ($error !== NULL && in_array($error['type'], [E_ERROR, E_PARSE, E_CORE_ERROR, E_COMPILE_ERROR])) {
            $this->logger->error('Shutdown Error: ' . $error['message'], $error);
            if (!headers_sent()) {
                $this->display_error_page('System Error');
            }
        }
    }

    public function get_last_error() {
        return $this->last_error;
    }

    private function display_error_page($title) {
        if (defined('DOING_AJAX')) {
            return;
        }

        include(AIMAGIC_PLUGIN_DIR . 'templates/error.php');
    }

    public function log_api_error($response, $context = []) {
        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            $this->logger->error('API Error: ' . $response->get_error_message(), array_merge([
                'error_code' => $response->get_error_code()
            ], $context));
            return true;
        }

        $response_code = wp_remote_retrieve_response_code($response);
        if ($response_code >= 400) {
            $this->logger->error('API Error: HTTP ' . $response_code, array_merge([
                'response' => wp_remote_retrieve_body($response)
            ], $context));
            return true;
        }

        return false;
    }

    public function handle_db_error($wpdb, $context = []) {
        if ($wpdb->last_error) {
            $this->logger->error('Database Error: ' . $wpdb->last_error, array_merge([
                'query' => $wpdb->last_query
            ], $context));
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
}

檔名：class-rate-limiter.php

<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class RateLimiter {
    private $cache_group = 'aimagic_rate_limits';
    private $default_limit = 1000; // requests per hour
    private $default_window = 3600; // 1 hour in seconds

    public function check($key, $limit = null, $window = null) {
        $limit = $limit ?: $this->default_limit;
        $window = $window ?: $this->default_window;

        $cache_key = $this->get_cache_key($key);
        $current = wp_cache_get($cache_key, $this->cache_group);

        if ($current === false) {
            wp_cache_add($cache_key, 1, $this->cache_group, $window);
            return true;
        }

        if ($current >= $limit) {
            return false;
        }

        wp_cache_incr($cache_key, 1, $this->cache_group);
        return true;
    }

    public function get_remaining($key, $limit = null) {
        $limit = $limit ?: $this->default_limit;
        $cache_key = $this->get_cache_key($key);
        $current = wp_cache_get($cache_key, $this->cache_group);

        if ($current === false) {
            return $limit;
        }

        return max(0, $limit - $current);
    }

    public function reset($key) {
        $cache_key = $this->get_cache_key($key);
        wp_cache_delete($cache_key, $this->cache_group);
    }

    private function get_cache_key($key) {
        return 'rate_limit_' . md5($key);
    }
}

檔名：class-error-handler (2).php

<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class ErrorHandler {
    private $logger;
    private $last_error;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->logger = new Logger();
        $this->last_error = null;
    }

    public function init() {
        set_error_handler([$this, 'handle_error']);
        set_exception_handler([$this, 'handle_exception']);
        register_shutdown_function([$this, 'handle_shutdown']);
    }

    public function handle_error($errno, $errstr, $errfile, $errline) {
        if (!(error_reporting() & $errno)) {
            return false;
        }

        $error_data = [
            'type' => $errno,
            'message' => $errstr,
            'file' => $errfile,
            'line' => $errline
        ];

        switch ($errno) {
            case E_USER_ERROR:
                $this->logger->error('Fatal Error: ' . $errstr, $error_data);
                $this->display_error_page('Fatal Error');
                exit(1);

            case E_USER_WARNING:
                $this->logger->warning('Warning: ' . $errstr, $error_data);
                break;

            case E_USER_NOTICE:
                $this->logger->notice('Notice: ' . $errstr, $error_data);
                break;

            default:
                $this->logger->error('Unknown Error: ' . $errstr, $error_data);
                break;
        }

        $this->last_error = $error_data;
        return true;
    }

    public function handle_exception($exception) {
        $error_data = [
            'type' => get_class($exception),
            'message' => $exception->getMessage(),
            'file' => $exception->getFile(),
            'line' => $exception->getLine(),
            'trace' => $exception->getTraceAsString()
        ];

        $this->logger->error('Uncaught Exception: ' . $exception->getMessage(), $error_data);
        $this->last_error = $error_data;

        if (defined('DOING_AJAX')) {
            wp_send_json_error([
                'message' => __('An unexpected error occurred.', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                'error' => $exception->getMessage()
            ]);
        } else {
            $this->display_error_page('System Error');
        }
    }

    public function handle_shutdown() {
        $error = error_get_last();
        if ($error !== NULL && in_array($error['type'], [E_ERROR, E_PARSE, E_CORE_ERROR, E_COMPILE_ERROR])) {
            $this->logger->error('Shutdown Error: ' . $error['message'], $error);
            if (!headers_sent()) {
                $this->display_error_page('System Error');
            }
        }
    }

    public function get_last_error() {
        return $this->last_error;
    }

    private function display_error_page($title) {
        if (defined('DOING_AJAX')) {
            return;
        }

        include(AIMAGIC_PLUGIN_DIR . 'templates/error.php');
    }

    public function log_api_error($response, $context = []) {
        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            $this->logger->error('API Error: ' . $response->get_error_message(), array_merge([
                'error_code' => $response->get_error_code()
            ], $context));
            return true;
        }

        $response_code = wp_remote_retrieve_response_code($response);
        if ($response_code >= 400) {
            $this->logger->error('API Error: HTTP ' . $response_code, array_merge([
                'response' => wp_remote_retrieve_body($response)
            ], $context));
            return true;
        }

        return false;
    }

    public function handle_db_error($wpdb, $context = []) {
        if ($wpdb->last_error) {
            $this->logger->error('Database Error: ' . $wpdb->last_error, array_merge([
                'query' => $wpdb->last_query
            ], $context));
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
}

檔名：class-webhook-handler.php
