<?php
namespace AIMagic;

class WebhookHandler {
    private $secret;
    private $logger;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->secret = get_option('aimagic_webhook_secret');
        $this->logger = new Logger();
    }

    public function init() {
        add_action('rest_api_init', [$this, 'register_webhook_endpoint']);
    }

    public function register_webhook_endpoint() {
        register_rest_route('aimagic/v1', '/webhook', [
            'methods' => 'POST',
            'callback' => [$this, 'handle_webhook'],
            'permission_callback' => [$this, 'verify_webhook_signature']
        ]);
    }

    public function verify_webhook_signature($request) {
        $signature = $request->get_header('X-Aimagic-Signature');
        if (!$signature) {
            $this->logger->error('Missing webhook signature');
            return false;
        }

        $payload = $request->get_body();
        $expected_signature = hash_hmac('sha256', $payload, $this->secret);

        if (!hash_equals($expected_signature, $signature)) {
            $this->logger->error('Invalid webhook signature');
            return false;
        }

        return true;
    }

    public function handle_webhook($request) {
        try {
            $payload = $request->get_json_params();
            
            if (!isset($payload['event']) || !isset($payload['data'])) {
                throw new \Exception('Invalid webhook payload format');
            }

            switch ($payload['event']) {
                case 'task.completed':
                    return $this->handle_task_completed($payload['data']);
                
                case 'task.failed':
                    return $this->handle_task_failed($payload['data']);
                
                case 'quota.exceeded':
                    return $this->handle_quota_exceeded($payload['data']);
                
                default:
                    throw new \Exception('Unknown webhook event: ' . $payload['event']);
            }
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $this->logger->error('Webhook error: ' . $e->getMessage());
            return new \WP_Error(
                'webhook_error',
                $e->getMessage(),
                ['status' => 400]
            );
        }
    }

    private function handle_task_completed($data) {
        global $wpdb;

        // Start transaction
        $wpdb->query('START TRANSACTION');

        try {
            // Update task status
            $updated = $wpdb->update(
                $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tasks',
                [
                    'status' => 'completed',
                    'result' => sanitize_textarea_field($data['result']),
                    'completed_at' => current_time('mysql'),
                    'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
                ],
                ['id' => intval($data['task_id'])],
                ['%s', '%s', '%s', '%s'],
                ['%d']
            );

            if ($updated === false) {
                throw new \Exception('Failed to update task status');
            }

            // Update quota usage
            $bytes_used = intval($data['bytes_used']);
            if ($bytes_used > 0) {
                $updated = $wpdb->query($wpdb->prepare(
                    "UPDATE {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants
                    SET quota_used = quota_used + %d,
                        updated_at = %s
                    WHERE id = (
                        SELECT tenant_id 
                        FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks 
                        WHERE id = %d
                    )",
                    $bytes_used,
                    current_time('mysql'),
                    intval($data['task_id'])
                ));

                if ($updated === false) {
                    throw new \Exception('Failed to update quota usage');
                }
            }

            // Send email notification
            $task = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
                "SELECT t.*, u.user_email 
                FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tasks t
                LEFT JOIN {$wpdb->users} u ON t.user_id = u.ID
                WHERE t.id = %d",
                intval($data['task_id'])
            ));

            if ($task && $task->user_email) {
                wp_mail(
                    $task->user_email,
                    __('Task Completed', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    sprintf(
                        __('Your task #%d has been completed. Click here to view the results: %s', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                        $task->id,
                        admin_url('admin.php?page=ai-magic-publisher-tasks&action=view&id=' . $task->id)
                    )
                );
            }

            $wpdb->query('COMMIT');
            
            $this->logger->info('Task completed successfully', ['task_id' => $data['task_id']]);
            
            return new \WP_REST_Response(['status' => 'success'], 200);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $wpdb->query('ROLLBACK');
            
            $this->logger->error('Task completion failed: ' . $e->getMessage(), [
                'task_id' => $data['task_id']
            ]);
            
            return new \WP_Error(
                'task_completion_failed',
                $e->getMessage(),
                ['status' => 500]
            );
        }
    }

    private function handle_task_failed($data) {
        global $wpdb;

        $updated = $wpdb->update(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tasks',
            [
                'status' => 'failed',
                'error_message' => sanitize_textarea_field($data['error']),
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['id' => intval($data['task_id'])],
            ['%s', '%s', '%s'],
            ['%d']
        );

        if ($updated === false) {
            $this->logger->error('Failed to update task status', [
                'task_id' => $data['task_id']
            ]);
            return new \WP_Error(
                'update_failed',
                'Failed to update task status',
                ['status' => 500]
            );
        }

        $this->logger->error('Task failed', [
            'task_id' => $data['task_id'],
            'error' => $data['error']
        ]);

        return new \WP_REST_Response(['status' => 'success'], 200);
    }

    private function handle_quota_exceeded($data) {
        global $wpdb;

        // Update tenant status
        $wpdb->update(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_tenants',
            [
                'status' => 'quota_exceeded',
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['id' => intval($data['tenant_id'])],
            ['%s', '%s'],
            ['%d']
        );

        // Send notification to admin
        $tenant = $wpdb->get_row($wpdb->prepare(
            "SELECT * FROM {$wpdb->prefix}aimagic_tenants WHERE id = %d",
            intval($data['tenant_id'])
        ));

        if ($tenant) {
            wp_mail(
                get_option('admin_email'),
                __('Quota Exceeded Alert', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                sprintf(
                    __('Tenant "%s" has exceeded their quota limit. Please review their usage and adjust the quota if needed.', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    $tenant->name
                )
            );
        }

        $this->logger->warning('Quota exceeded', [
            'tenant_id' => $data['tenant_id'],
            'quota_used' => $data['quota_used'],
            'quota_limit' => $data['quota_limit']
        ]);

        return new \WP_REST_Response(['status' => 'success'], 200);
    }
}

<?php
namespace AIMagic\Integrations;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

class GPT4Integration {
    private $api_key;
    private $api_endpoint;
    private $model;
    private $settings;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->settings = get_option('aimagic_settings', []);
        $this->api_key = $this->settings['api_keys']['openai'] ?? '';
        $this->api_endpoint = $this->settings['endpoints']['openai'] ?? 'https://api.openai.com/v1';
        $this->model = $this->settings['defaults']['model'] ?? 'gpt-4';
    }

    /**
     * Generate content using GPT-4
     */
    public function generate_content($prompt, $params = []) {
        if (empty($this->api_key)) {
            return new \WP_Error('no_api_key', __('GPT-4 API key is not configured.', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }

        $defaults = [
            'max_tokens' => $this->settings['limits']['max_tokens'] ?? 2048,
            'temperature' => $this->settings['defaults']['temperature'] ?? 0.7,
            'top_p' => 1,
            'frequency_penalty' => 0,
            'presence_penalty' => 0
        ];

        $params = wp_parse_args($params, $defaults);

        $response = wp_remote_post($this->api_endpoint . '/chat/completions', [
            'headers' => [
                'Authorization' => 'Bearer ' . $this->api_key,
                'Content-Type' => 'application/json'
            ],
            'body' => json_encode([
                'model' => $this->model,
                'messages' => [
                    ['role' => 'system', 'content' => 'You are a helpful content generation assistant.'],
                    ['role' => 'user', 'content' => $prompt]
                ],
                'max_tokens' => $params['max_tokens'],
                'temperature' => $params['temperature'],
                'top_p' => $params['top_p'],
                'frequency_penalty' => $params['frequency_penalty'],
                'presence_penalty' => $params['presence_penalty']
            ]),
            'timeout' => 30
        ]);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            return $response;
        }

        $body = json_decode(wp_remote_retrieve_body($response), true);

        if (!empty($body['error'])) {
            return new \WP_Error(
                'api_error',
                $body['error']['message'] ?? __('Unknown API error', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            );
        }

        return [
            'content' => $body['choices'][0]['message']['content'] ?? '',
            'usage' => $body['usage'] ?? [],
            'model' => $body['model'] ?? $this->model
        ];
    }

    /**
     * Test API connection
     */
    public function test_connection() {
        if (empty($this->api_key)) {
            return false;
        }

        $response = wp_remote_post($this->api_endpoint . '/chat/completions', [
            'headers' => [
                'Authorization' => 'Bearer ' . $this->api_key,
                'Content-Type' => 'application/json'
            ],
            'body' => json_encode([
                'model' => $this->model,
                'messages' => [
                    ['role' => 'user', 'content' => 'Test connection']
                ],
                'max_tokens' => 5
            ]),
            'timeout' => 10
        ]);

        return !is_wp_error($response) && wp_remote_retrieve_response_code($response) === 200;
    }
}

<?php
namespace AIMagic\Integrations;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

class LINEIntegration {
    private $channel_secret;
    private $channel_token;
    private $api_endpoint = 'https://api.line.me/v2';
    private $settings;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->settings = get_option('aimagic_settings', []);
        $this->channel_secret = $this->settings['line']['channel_secret'] ?? '';
        $this->channel_token = $this->settings['line']['channel_token'] ?? '';
    }

    /**
     * Verify webhook signature
     */
    public function verify_signature($signature, $body) {
        if (empty($this->channel_secret)) {
            return false;
        }

        $hash = base64_encode(hash_hmac('sha256', $body, $this->channel_secret, true));
        return hash_equals($signature, $hash);
    }

    /**
     * Send message to LINE
     */
    public function send_message($to, $messages) {
        if (empty($this->channel_token)) {
            return new \WP_Error('no_token', __('LINE Channel Access Token is not configured.', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }

        $response = wp_remote_post($this->api_endpoint . '/bot/message/push', [
            'headers' => [
                'Authorization' => 'Bearer ' . $this->channel_token,
                'Content-Type' => 'application/json'
            ],
            'body' => json_encode([
                'to' => $to,
                'messages' => $this->format_messages($messages)
            ]),
            'timeout' => 30
        ]);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            return $response;
        }

        $body = json_decode(wp_remote_retrieve_body($response), true);

        if (!empty($body['message'])) {
            return new \WP_Error('api_error', $body['message']);
        }

        return true;
    }

    /**
     * Format messages for LINE API
     */
    private function format_messages($messages) {
        if (!is_array($messages)) {
            $messages = [
                [
                    'type' => 'text',
                    'text' => $messages
                ]
            ];
        }

        foreach ($messages as &$message) {
            if (is_string($message)) {
                $message = [
                    'type' => 'text',
                    'text' => $message
                ];
            }
        }

        return $messages;
    }

    /**
     * Handle webhook events
     */
    public function handle_webhook($body) {
        $events = $body['events'] ?? [];
        $results = [];

        foreach ($events as $event) {
            switch ($event['type']) {
                case 'message':
                    $results[] = $this->handle_message_event($event);
                    break;
                case 'follow':
                    $results[] = $this->handle_follow_event($event);
                    break;
                case 'unfollow':
                    $results[] = $this->handle_unfollow_event($event);
                    break;
                default:
                    $results[] = new \WP_Error('unknown_event', 'Unknown event type: ' . $event['type']);
            }
        }

        return $results;
    }

    /**
     * Handle message event
     */
    private function handle_message_event($event) {
        $user_id = $event['source']['userId'] ?? '';
        $message = $event['message'] ?? [];

        if ($message['type'] !== 'text') {
            return $this->send_message($user_id, __('Sorry, I can only process text messages.', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }

        // Process the message through GPT-4
        $gpt4 = new GPT4Integration();
        $response = $gpt4->generate_content($message['text']);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            return $this->send_message($user_id, __('Sorry, I encountered an error processing your message.', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }

        return $this->send_message($user_id, $response['content']);
    }

    /**
     * Handle follow event
     */
    private function handle_follow_event($event) {
        $user_id = $event['source']['userId'] ?? '';
        
        // Get user profile
        $profile = $this->get_user_profile($user_id);
        if (!is_wp_error($profile)) {
            // Store user info in database
            $this->store_line_user($profile);
        }

        return $this->send_message($user_id, [
            [
                'type' => 'text',
                'text' => __('Thank you for following! I am your AI assistant. Feel free to ask me anything!', 'ai-magic-publisher')
            ],
            [
                'type' => 'template',
                'altText' => __('Get Started Menu', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                'template' => [
                    'type' => 'buttons',
                    'title' => __('Get Started', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    'text' => __('What would you like to do?', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                    'actions' => [
                        [
                            'type' => 'message',
                            'label' => __('Generate Content', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                            'text' => '/generate'
                        ],
                        [
                            'type' => 'message',
                            'label' => __('Help', 'ai-magic-publisher'),
                            'text' => '/help'
                        ]
                    ]
                ]
            ]
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Handle unfollow event
     */
    private function handle_unfollow_event($event) {
        $user_id = $event['source']['userId'] ?? '';
        
        // Update user status in database
        $this->update_line_user_status($user_id, 'unfollowed');
        
        return true;
    }

    /**
     * Get user profile from LINE
     */
    private function get_user_profile($user_id) {
        $response = wp_remote_get($this->api_endpoint . '/bot/profile/' . $user_id, [
            'headers' => [
                'Authorization' => 'Bearer ' . $this->channel_token
            ]
        ]);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            return $response;
        }

        return json_decode(wp_remote_retrieve_body($response), true);
    }

    /**
     * Store LINE user in database
     */
    private function store_line_user($profile) {
        global $wpdb;

        return $wpdb->replace(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_line_users',
            [
                'user_id' => $profile['userId'],
                'display_name' => $profile['displayName'],
                'picture_url' => $profile['pictureUrl'] ?? '',
                'status' => 'active',
                'created_at' => current_time('mysql'),
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['%s', '%s', '%s', '%s', '%s', '%s']
        );
    }

    /**
     * Update LINE user status
     */
    private function update_line_user_status($user_id, $status) {
        global $wpdb;

        return $wpdb->update(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_line_users',
            [
                'status' => $status,
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['user_id' => $user_id],
            ['%s', '%s'],
            ['%s']
        );
    }

    /**
     * Test API connection
     */
    public function test_connection() {
        if (empty($this->channel_token)) {
            return false;
        }

        $response = wp_remote_get($this->api_endpoint . '/bot/info', [
            'headers' => [
                'Authorization' => 'Bearer ' . $this->channel_token
            ],
            'timeout' => 10
        ]);

        return !is_wp_error($response) && wp_remote_retrieve_response_code($response) === 200;
    }
}

目錄：/www/wwwroot/xart004.heatgroups.top/wp-content/plugins/ai_plateform_v2/files_2025/includes/integrations
檔名：class-wechat-integration.php

<?php
namespace AIMagic\Integrations;

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

class WeChatIntegration {
    private $app_id;
    private $app_secret;
    private $token;
    private $access_token;
    private $api_endpoint = 'https://api.weixin.qq.com';
    private $settings;

    public function __construct() {
        $this->settings = get_option('aimagic_settings', []);
        $this->app_id = $this->settings['wechat']['app_id'] ?? '';
        $this->app_secret = $this->settings['wechat']['app_secret'] ?? '';
        $this->token = $this->settings['wechat']['token'] ?? '';
    }

    /**
     * Verify WeChat server signature
     */
    public function verify_signature($signature, $timestamp, $nonce) {
        if (empty($this->token)) {
            return false;
        }

        $arr = [$this->token, $timestamp, $nonce];
        sort($arr, SORT_STRING);
        $str = implode($arr);
        $calculated = sha1($str);

        return hash_equals($signature, $calculated);
    }

    /**
     * Get access token
     */
    private function get_access_token() {
        if ($this->access_token) {
            return $this->access_token;
        }

        // Try to get from cache first
        $cached = get_transient('aimagic_wechat_access_token');
        if ($cached) {
            $this->access_token = $cached;
            return $cached;
        }

        // Request new token
        $response = wp_remote_get($this->api_endpoint . '/cgi-bin/token', [
            'body' => [
                'grant_type' => 'client_credential',
                'appid' => $this->app_id,
                'secret' => $this->app_secret
            ]
        ]);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            return $response;
        }

        $body = json_decode(wp_remote_retrieve_body($response), true);

        if (!empty($body['errcode'])) {
            return new \WP_Error('wechat_error', $body['errmsg'], ['code' => $body['errcode']]);
        }

        $this->access_token = $body['access_token'];
        set_transient('aimagic_wechat_access_token', $this->access_token, $body['expires_in'] - 300);

        return $this->access_token;
    }

    /**
     * Send message to WeChat
     */
    public function send_message($to, $message) {
        $access_token = $this->get_access_token();
        if (is_wp_error($access_token)) {
            return $access_token;
        }

        $response = wp_remote_post($this->api_endpoint . '/cgi-bin/message/custom/send?access_token=' . $access_token, [
            'body' => json_encode([
                'touser' => $to,
                'msgtype' => 'text',
                'text' => [
                    'content' => $message
                ]
            ])
        ]);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            return $response;
        }

        $body = json_decode(wp_remote_retrieve_body($response), true);

        if (!empty($body['errcode']) && $body['errcode'] !== 0) {
            return new \WP_Error('wechat_error', $body['errmsg'], ['code' => $body['errcode']]);
        }

        return true;
    }

    /**
     * Handle webhook events
     */
    public function handle_webhook($xml) {
        $data = $this->parse_xml($xml);
        if (is_wp_error($data)) {
            return $data;
        }

        switch ($data['MsgType']) {
            case 'text':
                return $this->handle_text_message($data);
            case 'event':
                return $this->handle_event($data);
            default:
                return $this->create_reply($data, __('Sorry, this message type is not supported.', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }
    }

    /**
     * Handle text message
     */
    private function handle_text_message($data) {
        // Process the message through GPT-4
        $gpt4 = new GPT4Integration();
        $response = $gpt4->generate_content($data['Content']);

        if (is_wp_error($response)) {
            return $this->create_reply($data, __('Sorry, I encountered an error processing your message.', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }

        return $this->create_reply($data, $response['content']);
    }

    /**
     * Handle WeChat events
     */
    private function handle_event($data) {
        switch ($data['Event']) {
            case 'subscribe':
                return $this->handle_subscribe_event($data);
            case 'unsubscribe':
                return $this->handle_unsubscribe_event($data);
            default:
                return $this->create_reply($data, __('Event received.', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }
    }

    /**
     * Handle subscribe event
     */
    private function handle_subscribe_event($data) {
        // Store user info
        $this->store_wechat_user([
            'openid' => $data['FromUserName'],
            'status' => 'active'
        ]);

        return $this->create_reply($data, __(
            "Welcome to AI Magic Publisher! 🎉\n\n" .
            "I'm your AI assistant, ready to help you with content creation and more.\n\n" .
            "Try these commands:\n" .
            "- /generate - Generate new content\n" .
            "- /help - Get help and see all commands\n" .
            "- /status - Check your account status",
            'ai-magic-publisher'
        ));
    }

    /**
     * Handle unsubscribe event
     */
    private function handle_unsubscribe_event($data) {
        $this->update_wechat_user_status($data['FromUserName'], 'unsubscribed');
        return '';
    }

    /**
     * Create XML reply
     */
    private function create_reply($data, $content) {
        return "<xml>
            <ToUserName><![CDATA[{$data['FromUserName']}]]></ToUserName>
            <FromUserName><![CDATA[{$data['ToUserName']}]]></FromUserName>
            <CreateTime>" . time() . "</CreateTime>
            <MsgType><![CDATA[text]]></MsgType>
            <Content><![CDATA[{$content}]]></Content>
        </xml>";
    }

    /**
     * Parse incoming XML
     */
    private function parse_xml($xml) {
        libxml_disable_entity_loader(true);
        $data = simplexml_load_string($xml, 'SimpleXMLElement', LIBXML_NOCDATA);
        
        if ($data === false) {
            return new \WP_Error('xml_parse_error', __('Failed to parse XML', 'ai-magic-publisher'));
        }

        return json_decode(json_encode($data), true);
    }

    /**
     * Store WeChat user in database
     */
    private function store_wechat_user($data) {
        global $wpdb;

        return $wpdb->replace(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_wechat_users',
            array_merge($data, [
                'created_at' => current_time('mysql'),
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ]),
            ['%s', '%s', '%s', '%s']
        );
    }

    /**
     * Update WeChat user status
     */
    private function update_wechat_user_status($openid, $status) {
        global $wpdb;

        return $wpdb->update(
            $wpdb->prefix . 'aimagic_wechat_users',
            [
                'status' => $status,
                'updated_at' => current_time('mysql')
            ],
            ['openid' => $openid],
            ['%s', '%s'],
            ['%s']
        );
    }

    /**
     * Test API connection
     */
    public function test_connection() {
        if (empty($this->app_id) || empty($this->app_secret)) {
            return false;
        }

        $access_token = $this->get_access_token();
        return !is_wp_error($access_token);
    }
}
